var thinClientApiRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
    $.getJSON('config.json', function (config) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = shipExecServiceUrl.startsWith('http') ? { 'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem("TCToken")).access_token } : '';
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
    });
}
}

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {  
    if (location === '/shipping') {
       // debugger;
       
       // Get the Logon Profiles Custom Data Values Which Determine the Shipping Options Available to them
        if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === "undefined" || this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === null){
           throw ({ message: 'User Is Missing Required Custom Data Values in Management Studio User Manager Setup Under Address Tab.', errorCode: '' }); 
        }
     
        this.GetCustomDataItems();
            console.log(st_AddressType + ' ' + sf_AddressType + ' ' + uPS_Service + ' ' + return_Type + ' ' + user_description + ' ' + dims + ' ' + user_orderNumber + ' ' + cost_Center + ' ' + user_partNumber + ' ' + insured_Value);
        
        this.ShippingLoaded();
        
        var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
        {
            if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]'))) 
            {
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                $('#sf_Address').focus();
                $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#svc_select").prop("selectedIndex", 5);
            
                
            }
        }, 400);
        
        //Get Address Book Data
        var addressBookData = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            UserId: client.userContext.UserId
        };
        AddressBooks = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_AddressBook', addressBookData, false).responseJSON;
        AddressBooks.AddressBooks.forEach(item => {
            if(item.Name === "MULTI_ST"){
                shipToAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
            if(item.Name === "MULTI_SF"){
                shipFromAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
        });
        console.log("shipToAddressBookId: " + shipToAddressBookId);
        console.log("shipFromAddressBookId " + shipFromAddressBookId);    
        
        //Get the Shipper Account Number from Profile
        //this.GetShipperAccount(); 
        //console.log(thisShipperAccount);

        this.vm.shipToAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipToAddresses();
        //Setup Ship To Address Drop Down Change Event
       $('body').on('change', '#st_Address', function(e) {             // Not seeing a difference between using either of these as far as GUI reacts.
            var userSelectedShipToCompany = $('#st_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected ShipTo Company :" + userSelectedShipToCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedShipToCompany ==  ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedShipToAddress = ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateShipToAddress();
                }
            } 
            
            //Multi Profile only
            
            if(userSelectedShipToCompany == "BOSTON SCIENTIFIC COYOL"){
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "BS_26737";
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = "26737";
                //vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                //    Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED"
                //};
            }
            if(userSelectedShipToCompany == "BOSTON SCIENTIFIC HEREDIA"){
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "BS_26701";
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = "26701";
               // vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
               //     Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER"
               // };
            }
            
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
        });

        
        this.vm.returnAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipFromAddresses();
        //Setup Ship From Address Drop Down Change Event
        $('body').on('change', '#sf_Address', function(e) {
            //debugger;
            SelectedReturnAddress = null;
            var userSelectedReturnCompany = $('#sf_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected Return Company :" + userSelectedReturnCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedReturnCompany ==  ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedReturnAddress = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateReturnAddress();
                }
            } 
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
         
        });
        
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount"]', function(e){
             
            if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount > 2500 ){
                alert('ITN/AES Transaction Number Required');
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
                
            }
        });
        
        
       // $('#billWeight').after('<div id="billable_weight"><strong id="billable_weight_text"></strong></div>');
       // $('#volumetricWeight').after('<div id="custom_volumetric"><span id="volumetric_value_text"></span></div>');
       
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]', function(e){
            // debugger;
              totalShipWeight = 0;
              
              vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
              });
              
              totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
              //console.log(totalShipWeight);
             
              document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
         });
       
          $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]', function(e){
           
            totalVolumetricResult = 0;
           
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
            });
             totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
            //console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
         
            $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
         
            document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
            //debugger;
            if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
            {
                $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
                throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
            }
           
        });
       
    }
};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
     // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
     // debugger;
     
     totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
     
     //kg = lbs*0.453592    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments = vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// this.ShippingLoaded() // returns void
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (To Heredia or Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

// this.GetCustomDataItems() // returns void
this.GetCustomDataItems = function(){
    //debugger;
    userCustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
   
    st_AddressType = client.getValueByKey('Custom1',userCustomData);   
    sf_AddressType = client.getValueByKey('Custom2',userCustomData);  
    uPS_Service = client.getValueByKey('Custom3',userCustomData);        
    return_Type = client.getValueByKey('Custom4',userCustomData);            
    user_description = client.getValueByKey('Custom5',userCustomData);             
    dims = client.getValueByKey('Custom6',userCustomData);                   
    user_orderNumber = client.getValueByKey('Custom7',userCustomData);     
    cost_Center = client.getValueByKey('Custom8',userCustomData);        
    user_partNumber = client.getValueByKey('Custom9',userCustomData);     
    insured_Value = client.getValueByKey('Custom10',userCustomData);     
    
    
    
};

// Source: BULGARI (BULGARI)_Bulgari Reference Rules 2_1576.cs
// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        // debugger;
        this.vm.xReceiverAccountsIsHidden = true;
        this.vm.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressCodesIsHidden = true;


        this.vm.xReceiverAccounts = getReceiverAccounts();
        if (pageLoaded) {
            this.vm.xThirdPartyCode = tpbTransportationChargesAddressBookEntries;
        }
        //if (typeof shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress !== "undefined") shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Code = "";
    };

// this.ChangeTransportationCharges() // returns void
    this.ChangeTransportationCharges = function () {
        var shipmentRequest = this.currentShipment;
        var transportationCharges = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges;

        this.xReceiverAccountsIsHidden = transportationCharges != 'consignee';
        this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressCodesIsHidden = transportationCharges != 'thirdParty';

        this.xReceiverAccount = null;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = null;
        this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress = null;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress = null;
    }

// function defaultRateService() // returns void
    function defaultRateService() {
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var rateModalTable = $('table tbody[ng-repeat="rateResult in vm.rateResults"]');
            var rateModalServices = rateModalTable.find('tr td a');

            if (rateModalServices.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);

                rateModalServices.each(function (index, element) {
                    if ($(this).text() == 'UPS Second Day Air (UPS Adapter)') {
                        $(this).click();
                    }
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// GetAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) // returns array or undefined
    this.GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
            var addressBookEntry = { Code: 'Error: AddressBook "' + addressBookName + '" Not Found' };
            return [addressBookEntry];
        } else {
            var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
            searchCriteria = { OrderByClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", Direction: "asc", FieldType: 3 }] };
            data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries', data, false).responseJSON;
            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) {
                return response.AddressBookEntries;
            }
        }
    }

// GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
    function GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        if (customDataType === "To") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                if (fieldName.toUpperCase() === customField.Key.toUpperCase()) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;
    }

// SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// Source: Cabinet Works Group (MASCO)_Masco Client Side Business Rules_1752.cs
// function PreShip(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreShip = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}

// Source: Carrier Misroute (CMR) (CMR)_Client Business Rules_2487.cs
// function shipping() // returns void
function shipping () {
            vm.shipping = {
                panelMessage: '',
                loadValue: '[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]',
                notificationInterval: 1800000, //30 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 1200000, //20 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 5000, //5 seconds
                videoModal: {
                    selector: '#VideoModalId',
                    zoom: {
                        in: zoomIn,
                        out: zoomOut,
                    },
                    close: videoModalClose,
                    stream: {
                        selector: '#CameraStreamId',
                        start: videoStreamStart,
                        stop: videoStreamStop,
                        captureImage: captureImage
                    }
                },
                imageFile: {
                    selector: '#CarrierLabelImageId',
                    upload: uploadCarrierLabelFile
                },
                menu: {
                    guide: {
                        inputFile: {
                            selector: '#inputFileDownload',
                        }
                    }
                },
                load: loadShip,
                customerChange: customerChange,
                getNotification: getNotification,
                selectDownloadFile: selectDownloadFile
            }
            vm.shipping.videoModal.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.imageFile.id = vm.shipping.imageFile.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.id = vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector.substring(1);

            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.imageFile.selector, uploadCarrierLabelFile);
            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector, inputFileDownloadChange);

            vm.shipping.slic = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.profile.Name.substring(0,5) : vm.profile.Name == thinClient.adminProfileName ? "XXXXX" : null;
            vm.shipping.customers = getShipperCustomers(vm.profile.Shippers);
            var enabledCustomers = vm.shipping.customers.filter(function(c) { return c.disabled != true; });
            vm.shipping.customer = enabledCustomers.length == 1 ? vm.shipping.customers[1] : vm.shipping.customers[0];
            vm.shipping.activePanel = vm.shipping.slic == undefined || vm.clientContext.Machine.Name == undefined ? 0 : 1;

            debugger;

            vm.fieldOptions = {
                Consignee: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                },
                ReturnAddress: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                }
            };
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference18.IsDisabled = true;
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.DefaultValue = vm.shipping.slic;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = vm.shipping.slic;

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (!vm.profile.FieldOptions?.Reference?.IsHidden)
                    'form[name="referenceForm"] .panel > div'.unwrap();

                'name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="poBox.isHidden()"'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="residential.isHidden()"'.remove();


                vm.shipping.getNotification();
                thinClient.notificationIntervalId = setInterval(function() {
                    vm.shipping.getNotification();
                }, vm.shipping.notificationInterval);

                if (vm.shipping.customer.disabled)
                    vm.shipping.customer.selector.focus();
                else
                    vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
            }

            function getNotification() {
                var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id }
                thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                    if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications)) {
                        if (vm.clientContext.Site.Name == undefined)
                            vm.notification = null;
                        else {
                            var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id, SiteId: vm.clientContext.Site.Id };
                            thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                                if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications))
                                    vm.notification = null;

                                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                            })
                        }
                    }
                    vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                })

                this.setNotification = function(notifications) {
                    var notification = notifications.at(-1);
                    if (notification == undefined) return false;

                    this.notification = {
                        Title: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Title),
                        Message: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Message)
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            }

            function selectDownloadFile(event) {
                this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile = event.target.innerText;
                if (this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) {
                    if (this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile.slice(-3) == this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name.slice(-3))
                        updateFile();
                } else {
                    var payload = { Action: 'downloadFile', Data: this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile };
                    var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                            var data = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));

                            let linkData = `data:${data.fileType};base64,${data.encodedFile}`;
                            let downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            downloadLink.download = data.fileName;
                            downloadLink.href = linkData;
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                        }
                    });
                }

                function updateFile() {
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var request = {
                            Key: vm.shipping.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile,
                            Value: JSON.stringify({
                                fileType: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.type,
                                fileName: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name,
                                encodedFile: this.result.split(',')[1]
                            })
                        }
                        var payload = { Action: 'updateFile', Data: request };
                        var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                        thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                            if (ret.ErrorCode !== 0)
                                vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(ret.ErrorCode + " - " + ret.ErrorMessage);
                        }).catch(function (response) {
                            vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(vm.translations.Common.ErrorConnectingWCFService + ": " + response.status + " " + response.statusText);
                        })
                        vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = null;
                        $(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector).val(null);
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();

                    }
                    if (vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) reader.readAsDataURL(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected);
                }
            }

            function inputFileDownloadChange(event) {
                if (event.target.files == undefined) return;
                vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = event.target.files[0];
                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
            }

            function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

            function customerChange() {
                vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }


            function videoModalClose () {
                var $videoModal = $(vm.shipping.videoModal.selector);
                if ($videoModal.is(':visible'))
                    $videoModal.find('.close').click();
            }

            function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

            function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {
                //         var dataURL = reader.result;
                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                //             console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                //         });

                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                //         vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

            function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) {
                return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = fileData;
                    img.onload = function () {
                        var width = this.naturalWidth;
                        var height = this.naturalHeight;
                        console.log(`Image dimensions: ${width}x${height}`);
                        var megapixels = (width * height) / 1000000;
                        resolve(megapixels);
                    }
                })
            }

            function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }


            function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

            function zoomOut() {
                // localStorage.setItem("settings", JSON.stringify(userSettings));
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel > vm.videoModal.zoom.min) {
                    zoomLevel -= 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function zoomIn() {
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel < vm.videoModal.zoom.max) {
                    zoomLevel += 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function loadShip(shipmentRequest) {
                debugger;
                vm.load();
                if (vm.shipping.customer.autoShip) {
                    vm.intervalId = setInterval(function(shipmentRequest) {
                        console.log(shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment)
                        if (shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment) {
                            clearInterval(vm.intervalId);
                            // if(!(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option'))
                                vm.ship();
                        }
                    }, 20, shipmentRequest)
                }
            }
        }

// function getNotification() // returns void
function getNotification() {
                var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id }
                thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                    if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications)) {
                        if (vm.clientContext.Site.Name == undefined)
                            vm.notification = null;
                        else {
                            var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id, SiteId: vm.clientContext.Site.Id };
                            thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                                if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications))
                                    vm.notification = null;

                                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                            })
                        }
                    }
                    vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                })

                this.setNotification = function(notifications) {
                    var notification = notifications.at(-1);
                    if (notification == undefined) return false;

                    this.notification = {
                        Title: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Title),
                        Message: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Message)
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            }

// function getShipperCustomers(shippers) // returns array
function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

// function customerChange() // returns void
function customerChange() {
                vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }

// function uploadCarrierLabelFile() // returns void
function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

// function captureImage() // returns void
function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {
                //         var dataURL = reader.result;
                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                //             console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                //         });

                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                //         vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

// function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) // returns Promise
function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) {
                return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = fileData;
                    img.onload = function () {
                        var width = this.naturalWidth;
                        var height = this.naturalHeight;
                        console.log(`Image dimensions: ${width}x${height}`);
                        var megapixels = (width * height) / 1000000;
                        resolve(megapixels);
                    }
                })
            }

// function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) // returns void
function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }

// function videoStreamStart() // returns void
function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

// function zoomOut() // returns void
function zoomOut() {
                // localStorage.setItem("settings", JSON.stringify(userSettings));
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel > vm.videoModal.zoom.min) {
                    zoomLevel -= 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

// function zoomIn() // returns void
function zoomIn() {
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel < vm.videoModal.zoom.max) {
                    zoomLevel += 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

// function loadShip(shipmentRequest) // returns void
function loadShip(shipmentRequest) {
                debugger;
                vm.load();
                if (vm.shipping.customer.autoShip) {
                    vm.intervalId = setInterval(function(shipmentRequest) {
                        console.log(shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment)
                        if (shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment) {
                            clearInterval(vm.intervalId);
                            // if(!(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option'))
                                vm.ship();
                        }
                    }, 20, shipmentRequest)
                }
            }

// function PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        thinClient.loading.show();
        thinClient.dismiss.All();
        userParams.customer = this.vm.shipping.customer.value;
        userParams.labelImage = this.vm.labelImage;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15 = thinClient.today();
    }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        thinClient.loading.hide();
        this.vm.labelImage = null;


        if (this.vm.shipping.customer.value == 'AMAZON') {
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ConsigneeReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.IsDisabled = true;
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = true;

            if (this.vm.loadValue == 'Return') {
                this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = false;
                //this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
            }
        }

        if((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option')) {
            this.vm.shipping.activePanel = 0;
            this.vm.shipping.panelMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
        }
        this.vm.loadValue = null;
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        clearInterval(this.vm.intervalId);
        thinClient?.loading.hide();
        this.vm.shipping?.loadValue.focus();


        this.vm.labelImage = null;
        this.vm.shipping?.videoModal?.close();
        this.vm.showShipmentPanel = true

        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ConsigneeReference.IsDisabled = false;
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.IsDisabled = false;
        this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsDisabled = false;
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
 
      var shipment = GetShipment(shipmentRequest);

      shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (packageItem) {
         packageItem.ShipperReference = shipment.UserRef1;
         packageItem.ConsigneeReference = shipment.UserRef4;
      });

      function GetShipment(shipmentRequest) {

         class Shipment {
            constructor(shipmentRequest) {
               this.ShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
            }

            get UserRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User"); }
            get UserRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User"); }
            get UserRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User"); }
            get UserRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "User"); }
            get UserRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "User"); }
            get UserRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "User"); }
            get UserRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "User"); }
            get UserRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "User"); }
            get UserRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "User"); }
            get UserRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "User"); }

            get ToRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "To"); }
            get ToRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "To"); }
            get ToRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "To"); }
            get ToRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "To"); }
            get ToRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "To"); }
            get ToRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "To"); }
            get ToRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "To"); }
            get ToRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "To"); }
            get ToRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "To"); }
            get ToRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "To"); }

            GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
               var returnValue = "";
               var customData = null;
               if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
               if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

               if (customData) {
                  customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                     if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
                  })
               }
               return returnValue;
            }
         }
         return new Shipment(shipmentRequest);
      }
   };

// Source: Chrysler (Chrysler)_Chrysler Reference Rule_26.cs
// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        
        console.log('new shipment!');
        
        //Set the variable below equal to the name of the Custom Data field for this company
        var customDataName1 = "Custom1";
        var customDataName2 = "Custom2";
        
        var customSFValue1;
        var customSFValue2;
        
        var CustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        for(var SFCustom in CustomData){
            if(CustomData[SFCustom].Key==customDataName1)customSFValue1 = CustomData[SFCustom].Value;
            if(CustomData[SFCustom].Key==customDataName2)customSFValue2 = CustomData[SFCustom].Value;
        }
        
        var ref1;
        var ref2;
        
        //if null or undefined, set reference values to empty
        if(!customSFValue1)customSFValue1 = "";
        if(!customSFValue2)customSFValue2 = "";
        
        
        ref1 = customSFValue2;
        ref2 = customSFValue1;
        
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = ref1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = ref2;
    
        // Default Delivery Notification email to active user
		var userEmail = getUserEmail();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotification = true;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
        
    };

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined

      console.log('preship');
      console.log(shipmentRequest);
      for(var i =0;i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length;i++)
      {
          shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms;
      }
    }

// function getUserEmail() // returns userEmail
function getUserEmail(){
		var userEmail;
		var tmpstr = $("a[title='Manage']").text();
		userEmail = tmpstr.slice(6,-1);
		console.log(userEmail);
		
		if(userEmail != null)
		{
		   var trimspaces = userEmail.trim();
		   userEmail = trimspaces;
		}
		
		return userEmail;
	}

        var usCountry = "UNITED_STATES";
        var usAcronym = "US";
        var PackageRequests=shipmentRequest.Packages;
        
        $(PackageRequests).each(function (x, item)
          {
              var value = item.DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount;
              var tN = item.AesTransactionNumber;
              if (value >= 2500 && tN ===null)
              {
                    alert("Please check with clarios-na-trade@clarios.com if EEI filing is needed");
              }             
             item.Description=$('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
            
          });
          
          // For International Destination Rule Applies to all use cases and all carriers
          if ((shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usCountry) && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != usAcronym))
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "Y";
                }
                else
                {
                    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference8 = "N";
                }
             
    }

// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
      var DIUnit = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Units;
      var DIWt = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight.Amount;
      var DINote = "Incorrect shipping of Dry Ice can result in fines upward of $75,000 for each violation as well as cancellation of shipping privileges for all of Conagra Brands. Please contact DL-SmallParcelDeliveryService@conagra.com with questions or for specific instructions and restrictions";
   //   alert(DIUnit);
   //   alert(DIWt);
   //   alert(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DryIceWeight));
  for (var index = 0; index < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ++index) {

// function GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        if (cbr.historyShipment != null) {
            var historyRequest = JSON.parse(cbr.historyShipment);
            this.vm.totalPackages = historyRequest.Packages.length;

            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults = historyRequest.PackageDefaults;
            shipmentRequest.Packages = historyRequest.Packages;
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Description = "PC Equipment";

            shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {
                pkg.ReturnDelivery = true;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
                pkg.ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = historyRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
                pkg.Description = "PC Equipment";
            });
            cbr.historyShipment = null;
        }
        cbr.bulk.create.itemReferences = [];
    }

// getCustomData(nameAddress) // returns array
    function getCustomData(nameAddress) {
        if (nameAddress && nameAddress.CustomData) {
            return nameAddress.CustomData;
        }
        return [];
    }

// getKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
    function getKeyValue(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

// pad(num, size) // returns string
    function pad(num, size) {
    var s = "000000000" + num;
    return s.substr(s.length-size);
}

// userDataOnlyHistoryView(searchCriteria) // returns void
    function userDataOnlyHistoryView(searchCriteria) {
        var data_;
        data_ = GetUserContext_(data_);
        searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'UserId', FieldValue: data_.UserId, Operator: 0 });
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// this.PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

		}, 20);

		setTimeout(function() {
			clearInterval(alertInterval);
			clearInterval(labelInterval);
		}, 5000);
	};

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        var stName;
        var vmExists = false;

        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");

        if (typeof objVM === "undefined") {
            stName = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        } else {
            vmExists = true;
            stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
            objVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = isDefined(customData2) + "~" + stName;
        }
        // alert("customData2 = " + customData2);


        if (isDefined(customData3) == "FC") {
            if (vmExists === true) {
                objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            } else {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            }
            nameaddress.Account = isDefined(customData1);
        }

        function PullCustomData(consignee, field) {
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));

            for (var item in consignee) {
                if (consignee[item].Key == field) return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }

        function isDefined(referenceValue) {
            var goodValue = null;
            if (typeof referenceValue == "undefined" ||
                referenceValue === null) {
                goodValue = "";
            } else {
                goodValue = referenceValue;
            }
            return goodValue;
        }
    };

    };

// this.PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach(function (pkg) {

            pkg.MiscReference20 = vm.UserInformation.UserId;  
        });

        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            var sfState = getStateAbbreviation(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince);

                typeof sfState !== "undefined") {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = sfState;
