// this.AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns undefined
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = getShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
        function SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.ShipNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
    function SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) // returns undefined
    function SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, checked) {
        if (checked) {
            if (pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail == undefined || pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail.trim() == '') {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Origin;
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            } else {
                if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                    var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g');
                    if (!regexp.test(pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail)) {
                        pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Origin;
                    }
                } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                    pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail += ',' + emailAddress.Consignee;
                }
            }
        } else {
            var notificationAddressEmail = pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail;
            if (ngModelName == 'ShipToDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Consignee) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Consignee, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            } else if (ngModelName == 'ShipFromDeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail' && emailAddress.Origin) {
                var regexp = new RegExp(',?' + emailAddress.Origin, 'g')
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.replace(regexp, '');
            }

            if (notificationAddressEmail.indexOf(',') == 0) {
                notificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail.substring(1);
            }
            pkg.DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = notificationAddressEmail;
        }
    }

// function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) // returns emailAddress object
    function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) {
        var emailAddress = {}
        if (def.Consignee.Email != undefined && def.Consignee.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Consignee = def.Consignee.Email;
        }
        if (def.OriginAddress != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Origin = def.OriginAddress.Email;
        }
        return emailAddress;
    }

// function PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        
        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");
        
        var stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        
        if(customData3=="FC"){
            objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            nameaddress.Account = customData1;
        }
        
        
        function PullCustomData(consignee, field){
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));
            
            for(var item in consignee){
                if(consignee[item].Key==field)return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.consigneeCountryChange = this.ConsigneeCountryChange;
        var originCustomData = getCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = getKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = getKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
        setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee);
    };

// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince = getStateAbbreviation(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince);
//	debugger;
        //var branchNo = getKeyValue('Custom3', userCustomData)
		
		var branchNo = client.getValueByKey('Custom3', this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData);
		
        var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
        for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
            packages[i].MiscReference20 = branchNo;
            if (this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ProofRequireSignature || this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ProofRequireSignatureAdult) {
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Proof = true;
            }
            else {
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Proof = false;
            }
        }
    };

// PreSearchHistory(searchCriteria) // returns undefined
this.PreSearchHistory = function(searchCriteria) {
//        debugger;
        //var branchNo = getKeyValue('Custom3', userCustomData)
		var branchNo = client.getValueByKey('Custom3', this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData);
        if (branchNo) {
            searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'MiscReference20', FieldValue: branchNo, Operator: 5 });
        }
    }

// setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns undefined
function setInternationalPackaging(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
        var isInternational = nameAddress.Country != 'US';
        $('[property="Packaging"] select').prop('disabled', isInternational);
        if (isInternational) {
            var packages = shipmentRequest.Packages;
            for (var i = 0; i < packages.length; i++) {
                packages[i].Packaging = 'LETTER';
            }
        }
    }

// function singleCheckbox() // returns undefined
    function singleCheckbox() {
        var $checkbox = $(this);
        if ($checkbox.is(':checked') && $checkbox.is('[name]')) {
            // the name of the box is retrieved using the .attr() method
            // as it is assumed and expected to be immutable
            var group = 'input:checkbox[name="' + $checkbox.attr("name") + '"]';

            // the checked state of the group/box on the other hand will change
            // and the current value is retrieved using .prop() method
            $(group).prop('checked', false);
            $checkbox.prop('checked', true);
        }

    }

// Source: Epiq Bankruptcy Services (EPIQ)_Epiq CBR with UserContext Fix 2.0_1805.cs
// function CheckForRequiredValues() // returns boolean indicating whether required fields are valid
    function CheckForRequiredValues()
    {
      var bValid = true;

      if ($('#inputclient').val().trim().length == 0)
      {
        $('#inputclient').addClass('has-error');
        bValid = false;
        UIMethods.SwitchToTab(0);
      }

      /* If the 3rd party billing checkbox is checked, all the text fields need to be filled out. */
      if (($('#checkboxthirdparty').prop('checked') == true) && (bValid == true))
      {
        var textBoxes = $('#tabThirdPartyBilling input[type=text]');
        $(textBoxes).each(function(x, y)
        {
          if ($(this).val().trim().length == 0)
          {
            $(this).addClass('has-error');
            bValid = false;
            UIMethods.SwitchToTab(2);
          }
        });
      }

      return bValid;
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {

    if (location == '/shipping')
    {
      $(function()
      {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val('DOCUMENTS');
        $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"]').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'blur', function(e)
        {
          $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"] button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
        });
      });
    }

    if (location == '/batchmanager')
    {
      console.log(this.vm);
      console.log(this);
      $(document).ready(function()
      {
        $.globalEval('var userContext;');

        $('#batchUpdateTabs').delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
        {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopImmediatePropagation();
          e.stopPropagation();

          var i = $(this).attr('index');
          UIMethods.SwitchToTab(i);
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', function(e)
        {
          $(this).removeClass('has-error');
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkEditBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.EditThisBatch(this);
        });

        $('body').delegate('#checkboxthirdparty', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CheckForThirdPartyBilling();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.UpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCancelBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CancelUpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

      });
    }
  }

// CheckForRequiredValues() // returns boolean
    function CheckForRequiredValues()
    {
      var bValid = true;

      if ($('#inputclient').val().trim().length == 0)
      {
        $('#inputclient').addClass('has-error');
        bValid = false;
        UIMethods.SwitchToTab(0);
      }

      /* If the 3rd party billing checkbox is checked, all the text fields need to be filled out. */
      if (($('#checkboxthirdparty').prop('checked') == true) && (bValid == true))
      {
        var textBoxes = $('#tabThirdPartyBilling input[type=text]');
        $(textBoxes).each(function(x, y)
        {
          if ($(this).val().trim().length == 0)
          {
            $(this).addClass('has-error');
            bValid = false;
            UIMethods.SwitchToTab(2);
          }
        });
      }

      return bValid;
    }

// UpdateCurrentBatch() // returns false|void
      UpdateCurrentBatch: function()
      {
        if (CheckForRequiredValues() == false) { return false; }

        //var UserMethod = {};
        //UserMethod.ServerMethod = 'UpdateBatchData';

        var dataObject = {};

        dataObject.BatchReference = $('.batch-id').text();
        dataObject.Shipper = $('#selectshippers option:selected').val();
        dataObject.PackageType = $('#selectpackagetype option:selected').val();
        dataObject.DeliveryConfirmation = $('#checkboxdeliveryconfirmation').prop('checked');
        dataObject.SignatureRequired = $('#deliveryconfirmationcontainer input[type=radio]:checked').val();
        dataObject.BillingOption = $('#selectbilling option:selected').val();

        dataObject.Telephone = $('#inputphone').val();
        dataObject.PackageWeight = $('#inputweight').val();
        dataObject.PackageDeclaredValue = $('#inputdeclared').val();
        dataObject.Client = $('#inputclient').val();
        dataObject.GoodsDescription = $('#inputgoods').val();
        dataObject.ConsigneeAccount = $('#inputaccountnumber').val();

        dataObject.DomesticServiceMethod = $('#selectdomesticservice option:selected').val();
        dataObject.InternationalServiceMethod = $('#selectintlservice option:selected').val();
        dataObject.DomesticSaturday = $('#checkboxdomesticsaturdaydel').prop('checked');
        dataObject.DomesticInternational = $('#checkboxintlsaturdaydel').prop('checked');

        dataObject.ThirdPartyBilling = false;

        if ($('#checkboxthirdparty').prop('checked') == true)
        {
          /* Need to add 3rd party billing data. */
          dataObject.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCompany = $('#inputThirdPartyCompany').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyContact = $('#inputThirdPartyContact').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress1 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress1').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress2 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress2').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAddress3 = $('#inputThirdPartyAddress3').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCity = $('#inputThirdPartyCity').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyState = $('#inputThirdPartyState').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyPostalCode = $('#inputThirdPartyPostalCode').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyAccount = $('#inputThirdPartyAccount').val().trim();
          dataObject.ThirdPartyCountry = $('#selectThirdPartyCountry option:selected').val().replace("string:", "");
        }

        this.MakeUserMethodRequest('UpdateBatchData', dataObject).then(function() { $('#divCustomTabContainer').fadeOut(); });

        //UserMethod.MethodData = dataObject;
      }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {

    /* Don Beal (dbeal@ups.com) */
    /* 09-02-2021 */
    /* In the SE 1.x installation, the below are set */
    /*
      ship_req.packages[0].shipper_reference = ship_req.def_attr.consignee.company;
      ship_req.packages[0].misc_reference_1 = ship_req.def_attr.consignee.company;
      ship_req.packages[0].misc_reference_2 = ship_req.packages[0].consignee_reference;
    */

    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;

  }

// Source: F Schumacher (FSCHUMAC)_Product Area (8942X4) CBR with PV_1816.cs
// CheckWeightAndService(weightVal) // returns void
  function CheckWeightAndService (weightVal)
  {
    // /* Once the button is clicked, start a timer and wait for the weight to populate. */
    // /* If the weight is over 1 pound, switch the service from USPS FC to UPS Ground. */
    if ((weightVal > 1) && ($('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').find('option:selected').val() == "CONNECTSHIP_ENDICIA.USPS.FIRST"))
    {

      /* Deselect any currently selected options. */
      $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').val([]).scrollTop(10);

      /* Select the ground option. */
      $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"] > option[value="CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND"]')
        .prop({ 'selected': 'true', 'selected': true })
        .attr('selected', 'selected')
        .trigger('change').promise().done(function ()
        {

        });
    }
  }

// CheckForBasicErrors() // returns number
    function CheckForBasicErrors ()
    {
      var i = 0;
      /* Sometimes the weight OR service won't come across from the api, check for valid values and paint the invalid inputs red. */
      var weightInput = $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]');
      if (weightInput.val() == "") { $(weightInput).addClass('hasCustomError'); i += 1; }

      return i;
    }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');
          var a = {
            conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          var hdr = CustomerOrderObject.Header;
          var b = {
            conCompany: hdr.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: hdr.CONSIGNEE_ADDRESS_LINE_1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: hdr.CONSIGNEE_CITY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: hdr.CONSIGNEE_STATEPROVINCE.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: hdr.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          if (JSON.stringify(a) != JSON.stringify(b))
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + hdr.SHIPPER_REFERENCE + '. Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + hdr.SHIPPER_REFERENCE + '. Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          return (JSON.stringify(a) == JSON.stringify(b));
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      }

          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY": "US",
          "Order_Number": "50980336.4",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION": "DONT FRET",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_COMMENTS": null,
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFFCODE1": null,
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFCODE2": "",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_AVERAGEWEIGHT": 0.0
        */
        try
        {
          for (var x = 0; x < CommodityContents.length; x++)
          {
            /* Map the CommodityContent object here that will be used on the server.  By matching the structure here, hoping to push it straight to the viewmodel without any translation. */
            var CommodityObject = {
              UnitWeight: { Amount: "1" },
              Quantity: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY,
              ProductCode: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_PRODUCT_CODE,
              UnitValue: { Amount: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_UNIT_VALUE, Currency: 'USD' },
              QuantityUnitMeasure: GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY_UNIT_MEASURE),
              Description: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION,
              OriginCountry: (CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY.length > 0 ? CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY : 'US'),
              ConsigneePostalCode: (CommodityContents[x].CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE ? CommodityContents[x].CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.substring(0, 5) : null),
              EntryId: GetRandomNumber(8),
              OrderNumber: CommodityContents[x].Order_Number,
              HarmonizedCode: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFFCODE1,
              HarmonizedCode2: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFCODE2,
              AverageWeight: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_AVERAGEWEIGHT,
              UserData1: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_COMMENTS
            };

            $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails')
              .append($('<tr />').addClass('not-packed').attr('title', 'Order Number: ' + CommodityObject.OrderNumber)
                .append($('<td />').text(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_PRODUCT_CODE + ' ' + CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION))
                .append($('<td />').text(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY))
                .append($('<td />').text(0))
                .append($('<td />').text(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY))
                .append($('<td />').append('<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-plus trigger-icon add-box-item" title="Add this item to the current box." style="color: green;"></span>'))
                .data(CommodityObject))
              .promise().done(function ()
              {
                UpdateItemCounts();
                HideLoader();
              })
          }
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'AddCommoditiesToTable()', Error: error, Data: CommodityContents });
        }
      }

// ParseCutTicket(inVal) // returns void
      ParseCutTicket: function (inVal)
      {
        var splitArray = inVal.split(" ", 2);
        var itemNumber = splitArray[0];
        var itemQuantity = splitArray[1];
        var remainingQuantity, shippedQuantity;
        var matchingArray;

        try
        {
          /* Now find the table row that corresponds to the item number passed into the function. */
          var rowsArray = $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr.not-packed, tr.not-complete');

          matchingArray = $.grep(rowsArray, function (pVal, pIndex)
          {
            remainingQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(3)').text());
            shippedQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(2)').text());
            return (($(pVal).text().split(" ")[0] == itemNumber) && (itemQuantity == remainingQuantity));
          })[0];

          /* The matchingArray will contain rows that match the item needed with the quantity needed. */
          /* If the array is empty, find rows that have enough material to use. */
          if ($.isEmptyObject(matchingArray))
          {
            matchingArray = $.grep(rowsArray, function (pVal, pIndex)
            {
              remainingQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(3)').text());
              shippedQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(2)').text());
              return (($(pVal).text().split(" ")[0] == itemNumber) && (itemQuantity < remainingQuantity));
            })[0];
          }

          /* If the matchingArray is still empty, then the user tried to scan something into the box that wasn't part of the order.  Raise an error. */
          if ($.isEmptyObject(matchingArray))
          {
            this.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: Item ' + itemNumber + ' not found within currently loaded order(s).');
            return false;
          }

          $(matchingArray).data().ScanQuantity = itemQuantity;
          $(matchingArray).data().ItemNumber = itemNumber;

          this.AddRowItemToCurrentBox(matchingArray);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'ParseCutTicket()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// AddRowItemToCurrentBox(triggerElement) // returns void
      AddRowItemToCurrentBox: function (triggerElement)
      {
        try
        {
          var tableRow = $(triggerElement).closest('tr');
          var commodityContent = $(tableRow).data();

          /* No box type selected, paint the border red. */
          // if ($('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex') === 0)
          // {
          //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').css('border-color', 'crimson');
          // }

          /* This adds the commodities to the 'Goods' tab. */
          var packageIndex = $('span.current-container-index').text();
          packageIndex -= 1;
          this.AddCommoditiesToPackage(packageIndex, commodityContent);

          var newRow = $('<tr />').css('display', 'none');
          var itemDescText = $(tableRow).find('td:eq(0)').text();
          var itemNumber = itemDescText.split(' ')[0];
          var tableCurrent = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible');

          var trData = {};
          trData.OrderNumber = commodityContent.OrderNumber;
          trData.ItemNumber = itemNumber;
          trData.ItemDescription = itemDescText;
          trData.StartVal = parseFloat($(tableRow).find('td:eq(1)').text());
          trData.ShippedVal = parseFloat(commodityContent.ScanQuantity);
          trData.RemainingVal = parseFloat(trData.StartVal - trData.ShippedVal);
          trData.TotalVal = trData.ShippedVal;

          /* For the total value, find each entry with the same item# and total the values and add the shipped value. */
          $(tableCurrent).find('tr:gt(0)').find('td:eq(1)').each(function (e)
          {
            if ($(this).text() == trData.ItemNumber)
            {
              trData.TotalVal += parseFloat($(this).closest('tr').find('td:eq(2)').text());
            }
          });

          /* Both html tables will have data objects on the tr's. */
          /* Make the .EntryId element inside each tr data() object equal so it serves as a key between the two tables. */
          trData.EntryId = $(tableRow).data().EntryId;

          $(newRow).append($('<td />').text(commodityContent.OrderNumber))
            .append($('<td />').text(itemNumber))
            .append($('<td />').text(trData.ShippedVal))
            .append($('<td />').text(trData.TotalVal))
            .append($('<td />').append('<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-minus trigger-icon" title="Remove this item from the current box." style="color: crimson;"></span>'))
            .data(trData);

          /* If the destination table (container) is empty, get rid of the single '.empty-table' row. */
          // if ($('tr.empty-table').is(':visible'))
          // {
            $('tr.empty-table').fadeOut().promise().done(function ()
            {
              $(tableCurrent).append($(newRow).fadeIn().show()).promise().done(function (e) { UpdateItemCounts(); });
            });
          // }
          // else
          // {
          //   $(tableCurrent).append($(newRow).fadeIn().show());
          // }

          /* Now update the classes and amounts from the incoming order data (table on left side of screen). */
          /* We can link the source and destination order by using the .EntryKey data() element. */

          /* Update the shipped quantity. */
          var previouslyShipped = parseFloat($(tableRow).find('td:eq(2)').text());

          var a, b;
          a = parseFloat(commodityContent.ScanQuantity) + parseFloat(previouslyShipped);
          b = parseFloat(trData.StartVal) - a;

          $(tableRow).find('td:eq(2)').text(a);
          $(tableRow).find('td:eq(3)').text(b);

          var trCount = ($('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr').length - 1);

          /* Update the shipped amount, change the color to green. */
          /* Set Shipped value to the value of the 2nd td. */
          if ($(tableRow).find('td:eq(3)').text() > 0)
          {
            $(tableRow).removeClass('not-packed').addClass('not-complete');

            // /* If there is only a single row then change the class and return. */
            // if (trCount > 1)
            // {
            //   var insertTargetRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr.packed').first();
            //   if (insertTargetRow.length === 0)
            //   {
            //     insertTargetRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr.not-packed').last();
            //     //$(tableRow).detach().insertAfter(insertTargetRow);
            //   }
            //   else
            //   {
            //     //$(tableRow).detach().insertBefore(insertTargetRow);
            //   }
            // }
          }
          else
          {
            $(tableRow).removeClass('not-complete not-packed').addClass('packed').promise().done(function () { UpdateItemCounts(); });
            /* Change the icon, don't allow a click. */
            $(tableRow).find('td:eq(4) > span').removeClass('glyphicon-plus add-box-item').addClass('glyphicon-ban-circle').css('color', 'crimson').attr({ 'title': '' });

            // if (trCount > 1)
            // {
            //   /* Now move the row we just added to the box to the end of the list. */
            //   var lastRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').last();
            //   //$(tableRow).detach().insertAfter(lastRow);
            // }
          }

          this.CheckForCompletedPacking();

          /* If the user clicked on the last row of the table, don't need to detach and append it.  Exit here. */
          //if ($(tableRow).index() == ($(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').length - 1)) { return; }

          // if ($(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').length > 2)
          // {
          //   /* Now move the row we just added to the box to the end of the list. */
          //   var lastRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').last();
          //   $(tableRow).detach().insertAfter(lastRow);
          // }
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error});
        }
      }

// AddOrderNumbersToList() // returns void
      AddOrderNumbersToList: function ()
      {
        var inVal = $('#textOrderNumber').val();
        var bExists;

        /* Do not add duplicate entries to the select box. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').find('option').each(function ()
        {
          if (this.text == inVal)
          {
            bExists = true;
            /* Break out of the .each loop. */
            return false;
          }
        });

        if (bExists == true)
        {
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
          return false;
        }

        if (inVal.length > 0)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').append($('<option />')
            .val(inVal)
            .text(inVal)
            .trigger('change'))
            .promise().done(function ()
            {
              $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
            });
        }
      }

// SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers() // returns void
      SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers: function ()
      {
        try
        {
          /* Append the shipper reference with each item in the select list in csv format. */
          /* Once this is done, change the SSBR on post load to loop through each option in the csv list. */
          var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
          var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val();

          /* If the user closes the dialog box, then opens it back up, we don't want to check the same orders more than once so only process what was entered into the dialog box this time. */
          var ordersToQuery = '';

          /* Loop through all the orders in the select box and determine if they are already in the list. */
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').find('option').each(function (i, v)
          {
            /* Remove the spaces before the commas for comparison. */
            var arrayOrders = shipperReferenceVal.split(",").map(function (item)
            {
              return item.trim();
            });

            /* If the current option value is NOT in the list within the Shipper Reference field, add it. */
            if ($.inArray(v.value.trim(), arrayOrders) == -1)
            {
              ordersToQuery += v.value.trim() + ',';
              //shipperReferenceVal += ',' + v.value;
            }

            /* Remove the option once it is added to the input box. */
            $(this).remove();

          }).promise().done(function ()
          {
            /* Done creating the list of orders to get from the server which is now held in the ordersToQuery variable. */

            /* Hide the div. */
            $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

            /* Make sure there are orders in the list. */
            if (ordersToQuery.length > 0)
            {
              PackVerify.GetOrderInformationFromCustomer(ordersToQuery);
            }
            else
            {
              PackVerify.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: No unique orders to pull from the server.  All consolidated orders have already been added to this shipment.');
            }
          });
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderNumber) // returns void
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        //shipperReferenceVal += ',' + OrderNumber;

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(shipperReferenceVal);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(shipperReferenceVal);
        $('span.order-number-list').text(shipperReferenceVal);
      }

// GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(sVal) // returns string
    function GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement (sVal)
    {
      switch (sVal.toUpperCase())
      {
        case "EACH":
          return "EA";
        case "YARDS":
        case "YARD":
          return "YD";
        case "METER":
          return "M";
        case "SF":
          return "SFT";
        case "PAIR":
          return "PR";
        case "SR":
          return "ROL";
        default:
          return sVal;
      }
    }

// Source: F Schumacher (FSCHUMAC)_Product Area (8942X4) CBR_1801.cs
// WaitForElement(element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns Promise<void>
      WaitForElement: async function(element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        let a = await Tools.PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function(promiseResult)
        {
          if (defaultValue) { $(element).val(defaultValue); }

          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

          if (waitThenFocus == true) { $(element).focus(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          console.log('WaitForElement()', error);

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      },

// GetUniqueArrayFromString(inString, stringDelimiter) // returns string[]
      GetUniqueArrayFromString: function(inString, stringDelimiter = ',')
      {
        var trimArray = $.grep(inString.split(stringDelimiter), function(a)
        {
          return a.trim().length > 0;
        });

        /* Get rid of any duplicate array entries. */
        trimArray = trimArray.filter((e, i, a) => a.indexOf(e) === i);
        return trimArray;
      },

// GetUniqueCSVStringFromArray(inArray) // returns string
      GetUniqueCSVStringFromArray: function(inArray)
      {
        /* Get rid of any duplicate array entries. */
        var uniqueArray = inArray.filter((e, i, a) => a.indexOf(e) === i);
        var newUniqueString = '';

        $(uniqueArray).each(function(a, b)
        {
          if (b.trim().length > 0)
          {
            newUniqueString += b.trim() + ',';
          }
        });

        return newUniqueString;
      },

// GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(inString) // returns string
      GetUniqueCSVStringFromString: function(inString)
      {
        var uniqueArray = this.GetUniqueArrayFromString(inString, undefined);
        return this.GetUniqueCSVStringFromArray(uniqueArray);
      },

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function(CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');
          var a = {
            conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          var hdr = CustomerOrderObject.Header;
          console.log(hdr);
          var b = {
            conCompany: hdr.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: hdr.CONSIGNEE_ADDRESS_LINE_1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: hdr.CONSIGNEE_CITY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: hdr.CONSIGNEE_STATEPROVINCE.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: hdr.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            console.log(`CheckForMatchingConsignee(), Message: Could not add order ${CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber} (${CustomerOrderObject.orderId}). Primary order data to follow.`);
            console.log('Primary order: ', a);
            console.log('Secondary order: ', b);
          }

          return aa == bb;
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          console.log(error.message);
        }
      },

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    ConsolidatedOrders.InitElements(false);
    Tools.HideLoader();
    
    $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3);

    $('[ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function () 
    {
      /* Set the default box type to 'BAG 1'.  The multiple props and attr are for older browsers. */
      $('select[property="BoxType"] > option[label="SAMPLE BAG 1"]').prop({ 'selected': 'true', 'selected': true }).attr('selected', 'selected').trigger('change');

    });    
  }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val();
    // Tools.GetPackageDefaultsObject().UserData3 = $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked');
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3 = $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked');
  }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean or undefined on error
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');

          let a = {
            //conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ',''),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          let b = {
            //conCompany: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ', ''),
            conAddress1: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: CustomerOrderObject.shipCity.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: CustomerOrderObject.shipState.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: CustomerOrderObject.shipZipCode.trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          return (aa == bb);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      }

      {
        /* Reset the rate shopping checkbox. */
        $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked', false);
      }

// Source: FalconNDX (FNDX)_Falcon_CBR_1794.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        debugger;
        
        //Days List
        const days = ["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"];
         
        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
      
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
   this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
      var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference   = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
      // shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = "Ground";
   };

// function GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
   function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
      for (var index in arr) {
          if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
      }
      return '';
  }

//START

/*get user context data */
function GetUserContext(userContext) {
    if (userContext === undefined) {
        userContext = ajaxGet('api/usercontext/GET');
    }
    return userContext;
}

function ajaxGet(url) {
    var result;
    $.ajax({
        type: "GET",
        url: url,
        async: false,
        success: function(response) {
            result = response;
        }
    });
    return result;
}

//segregate user data by userid(so by default, users will only see their own account)
function userDataOnlyHistoryView(searchCriteria)
{
    var userContext;
    userContext = GetUserContext(userContext);
    searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'UserId', FieldValue: userContext.UserId, Operator: 0 });
}

//Shipexec function
this.PreSearchHistory = function (searchCriteria) {
    userDataOnlyHistoryView(searchCriteria);
};


//END
    
}

// GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
    function GetCustom(shipmentRequest, fieldName, customDataType) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        if (customDataType === "To") customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                if (fieldName.toUpperCase() === customField.Key.toUpperCase()) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;
    }

// SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// getAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) // returns array|undefined
    function getAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        debugger;
        //var response = ajaxPost('GetAddressBooks', data);
        var response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false);
        debugger;
        if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
            var addressBookEntry = { Code: 'Error: AddressBook "' + addressBookName + '" Not Found' };
            return [addressBookEntry];
        } else {
            var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;

            searchCriteria = { OrderByClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", Direction: "asc", FieldType: 3 }] };
            data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            //response = ajaxPost('GetAddressBookEntries', data);
            response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false);
            debugger;
            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) {
                return response.AddressBookEntries;
            }
        }
    }

// GetCustomData(nameAddress) // returns array
    function GetCustomData(nameAddress) {
        if (nameAddress && nameAddress.CustomData) {
            return nameAddress.CustomData;
        }
        return [];
    }

// GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
    function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

// Source: FortessaTS (FTS)_FortessaCBR_1897.cs
// customGetWeight() // returns void
        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

// replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) // returns void
        function replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                client.shipping.$selectBoxType = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]');
                if (client.shipping.$selectBoxType.length > 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType = $('<input type="text" />').attr({ class: client.shipping.$selectBoxType.attr('class') });
                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.hide();
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.insertAfter(client.shipping.$selectBoxType);

                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.keyup(boxTypes, function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                            for (var boxType of e.data) {
                                if (boxType.Name == this.value) {
                                    this.value = '';
                                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.val(boxType.Id).change();
                                    client.shipping.addPackageButton.focus();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            }, 10);
        }

// pastDueDate(miscReference6) // returns boolean
        function pastDueDate(miscReference6) {
            //if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0 && miscReference6 != '*1900-01-01T00:00:00*') {

            if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0) {

                miscReference6 = miscReference6.replaceAll('*', '');
                client.shipping.arriveByDate = miscReference6.split("T")[0];

                var dateRequired = Date.parse(miscReference6);
                if (dateRequired <= Date.now() && miscReference6 != "1900-01-01T00:00:00") {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-success').addClass('text-danger');
                    return true;
                }
                else {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').addClass('text-success');
                }
            };
            return false;
        }

// checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) // returns void
        function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 6;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						//var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
						viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
						shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
						//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

// addDays(days) // returns Date
        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
			
			console
            return date;
        }

// checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel) // returns void
        function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;
			var hardCutoffTime = 16;
			var currentDateTime = new Date();
			var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();
			
			if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
				var finalDate = addDays(2);
				console.log("New date" + finalDate);
				var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
				var day = finalDate.getDate();
				var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
				console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
				//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
				var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
				viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
				else{
					var finalDate = addDays(1);
					console.log("New date" + finalDate);
					var month = finalDate.getMonth() + 1;
					var day = finalDate.getDate();
					var year = finalDate.getFullYear();
					console.log("Month " + month + " Day " + day + " Year " + year);
					//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 30, Year: 2024 }
					var shipDate = {Month: month, Day: day, Year: year};
					viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
					shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
				}
				
			}
			
		}

// checkAndSetCPD(viewModel) // returns void
        function checkAndSetCPD(viewModel) {
            //create interval here to watch for CPD checkbox
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $cpdCB = $('[ng-model="vm.cpdProcessFlow"]');

                if ($cpdCB.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    var cpdFlag = sessionStorage.getItem("cpdflag");
                    //status can be True, False or Null

                    if (cpdFlag == "true") {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = false;
                    }


                }
            }, 10)

        }

// checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) // returns void
        function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 10;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

// addDays(days) // returns Date
        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
            return date;
        }

vm.Gap_PoolerCheckboxClick= function()

                    {
                        $("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.deliverDate.value\"]").val("2099-01-01").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        //$("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference\"]").val("Pool Carrier").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        //$("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference\"]").val(vm.profile.Shippers[0].Email.replace("@", "").replace(" ", "").replace(".pool", "").replace(".POOL", "")).trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        $("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount\"]").val("5").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        $("#dateDiv").hide();
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        $("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.deliverDate.value\"]").val("").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        $("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference\"]").val("").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        $("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference\"]").val("").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        $("input[type=text][ng-model=\"vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount\"]").val("").trigger("input").trigger("change");
                        $("#dateDiv").show();
                    }
                }

// this.GetShipToAddressCustomData() // returns custom data from the first address book entry
this.GetShipToAddressCustomData = function(){
        //debugger;
        var payloadShipToAddress = {
            "Skip": 0,
            "Take": 10,
            "WhereClauses": [{
                "FieldName": "Id",
                "FieldValue": consigneeId,
                "Operator": 0
            }]
        };
        
        var data = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            addressBookIds: addrsBookId,
            SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
        };
        //console.log(data);
      
        ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;
    
        console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData);
        
        return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[0].CustomData;
                
    };

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        debugger;
        const st_company = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company.toUpperCase();
        addrsBookId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBookId;
        consigneeId = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Id;
        
        if(st_company == "UPS MI" || st_company.includes("MAIL INNOVATIONS"))
        {
            console.log("Mail Innovatoins Shipment");
            console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.AddressBook);
            console.log(addrsBookId);
            console.log(consigneeId);
                
            addressCustomData = this.GetShipToAddressCustomData();
            mi_flag = client.getValueByKey('Custom1',addressCustomData);
                  
            if(mi_flag !== "MI_TPB"){
               throw new Error("Please contact GAP ShipExec Admin for Mail Innovation Authorization [Ship-Exec-stores-dg@gap.com].");
            }
            else
            {
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = {
                    Company : "UPS Mail Innovations",
                    Contact : "Shipping",
                    Address1 : "13050 Marlay Ave",
                    Address2 : "Suite 100",
                    City : "Fontana",
                    StateProvince : "CA",
                    PostalCode : "92337",
                    Country : "US",
                    Email : "upsusmi01transportation@ups.com",
                    Account : "7500YW"
                };
                      
            }
        }

        if (pooler)
        {
            if (document.getElementById("pooler").checked)
            {
                for (var p of shipmentRequest.Packages)
                {
                    p.MiscReference4 = vm.profile.Shippers[0].Email.replace("@", "").replace(" ", "").replace(".pool", "").replace(".POOL", "").toUpperCase();
                }               
            }
        }

        var misc3reference = "200.30.6035.5102.90059";
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = "";
            //Address 1
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "1112 Turkey Mountain Rd.")
            {
                console.log('found 1/4 address');
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;
            }
             //Address 2
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "102R Demi Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
              //Address 3
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "17511 S. Susana Rd.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
               //Address 4
            if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1 == "200 Terminal St.")
            {
                                console.log('found 1/4 address');

                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = misc3reference;
                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

            }
        }
        console.log('PRESHIP');
        console.log(shipmentRequest);

    };

                                shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = misc3reference;

// function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() // returns void
    function selectCanadaForAllCountrySelects() {
        // Check if the flag is already true, which means we no longer need to change the selects
        if(canadaSelected || !isSelectedValueInShippersArray()) {
          return; // Exit the function if Canada has been selected in all dropdowns or if the site is not from Canada
        }
        
        // Get all select elements with the name 'Country'
        var selects = document.querySelectorAll('select[name="Country"]');
        var allSelected = true; // To keep track if all selects have been set to Canada
      
        // Iterate through the NodeList
        selects.forEach(function(select) {
          // Only set the value to 'string:CA' if it's not already set
          if (select.value !== 'string:CA') {
            select.value = 'string:CA';
            allSelected = false; // Not all selects have been set to Canada
      
            // Trigger change event for AngularJS
            if ('createEvent' in document) {
              var evt = document.createEvent('HTMLEvents');
              evt.initEvent('change', false, true);
              select.dispatchEvent(evt);
            } else {
              select.fireEvent('onchange');
            }
          }
        });
      
        // If all selects have been set to Canada, set the flag to true
        if (allSelected) {
          canadaSelected = true;
        }
      }

// function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() // returns boolean
      function isSelectedValueInShippersArray() {
        // Use a more specific selector that targets the ng-model
        var selectElement = document.querySelector('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]');
        
        // Ensure the element exists
        if (!selectElement) {
          console.warn('Select element not found');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the index of the selected option
        var selectedIndex = selectElement.selectedIndex;
        
        // Ensure an option is selected
        if (selectedIndex < 0) {
          console.warn('No option is selected');
          return false;
        }
        
        // Get the selected option element
        var selectedOption = selectElement.options[selectedIndex];
        
        // Get the value of the selected option (and remove the "string:" prefix if present)
        var selectedValue = selectedOption.value.replace('string:', '');
        
        // Check if the selected value is in the array
        return StoreLocationsCanadaArray.includes(selectedValue);
      }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
       var shipment = new Shipment(shipmentRequest);  
       shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = shipment.UserRef1;

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
      if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }

// function AddMultiPackagesReal() // returns undefined
  function AddMultiPackagesReal()
  {
    var NumberPackage = $("#NumberPackage").val();
    if (NumberPackage === null || NumberPackage === "")
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Number Package is required")
      return;
    }
    for (var i = 0; i < NumberPackage; i++)
    {
      var elem = $('#duplicate');
      elem.click();
    }

    $("#NumberPackage").val("");
    MultiCloseModal();

  }
