// function SetUserData(shipmentRequest, isOptimalAccepted) // returns shipmentRequest
function SetUserData(shipmentRequest,isOptimalAccepted = false)
    {
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = $("#ddlShippingCharge").val();
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData2 = $("#ddlIsTobaccoShipment").val();
         var $loadValue = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
         if ($loadValue.length) {
             shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3 = $loadValue.val();
         }
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 = isOptimalAccepted;
         return shipmentRequest;
    }

// Source: Memorial Sloan-Kettering Cancer Center  (MSKCC)_MSKCC_Reference_Rules_63.cs
// getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) // returns an emailAddress object with Consignee/Origin fields when present
function getShipmentEmailAddresses(def) {
        var emailAddress = {}
        if (def.Consignee.Email != undefined && def.Consignee.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Consignee = def.Consignee.Email;
        }
        if (def.OriginAddress != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != undefined && def.OriginAddress.Email != '') {
            emailAddress.Origin = def.OriginAddress.Email;
        }
        return emailAddress;
    }

// Source: Meta Platforms (API Shipping) (METAPLATFORMSAPISHIPPING)_Meta Thin Client Profile CBR_1868.cs
// this.PostRate(shipmentRequest, rateResults) // returns void
    this.PostRate = function(shipmentRequest, rateResults) 
    {   
        const dateToday = new Date();

        var selectedDeliverDate = this.vm.deliverDate;

        LogRateInformationToConsole(shipmentRequest, rateResults);
        if (!shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) 
        {
            ApplyRulesWithoutServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday);
        }
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) 
        {
            ApplyRulesWithServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday);
        }
        if (rateResults)        
        {
            var ratedServiceArrivalDateString = GetArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);
            var ratedServiceArrivalAsDate = stringToDate(ratedServiceArrivalDateString, dateFormat, "-");    
            var expectedDeliveryDate = stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-");
            if (expectedDeliveryDate <= ratedServiceArrivalAsDate)
            {
                $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(formatDate(ratedServiceArrivalAsDate)).change();   
            }
        }
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) 
    {            
        //Services configured in Pending Shipments Profile Field Options
        var backup2DADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17; //UPSAPI.UPS.2DA        
        var backupNDADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; //UPSAPI.UPS.NDA        
        var backupExpeditedIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED        
        var backupExpressIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS        

        $('body').on('click', 'table[aria-describedby="Pending Shipments"] input[type="button"]', this.vm, 
        function(e) 
        {
            $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference5).change();
            if (e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service) 
            {
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference8"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').val(backup2DADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]').val(backupNDADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]').val(backupExpeditedIntlService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').val(backupExpressIntlService).change();
            }
        });
    };

// function ApplyRulesWithoutServiceRequested(shipmentRequest, rateResults, dateToday) // returns void
    function ApplyRulesWithoutServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday)
    {            
        if (stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-") <= dateToday) 
            {
                $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(formatDate(getTomorrowDate())).change();

                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val(formatDate(getTomorrowDate())).change();
            } 
            else if (rateResults) 
            {                
                var fullArriveDate = GetArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);

                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val(fullArriveDate).change();
            }   
    }

// function UpdateFields(dateValue, applyBackupService) // returns void
    function UpdateFields(dateValue,applyBackupService)
    {
        $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val(dateValue).change();
        
        if(applyBackupService)
        {
            $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(formatDate(getTomorrowDate())).change();
        }
        
    }

// function BackupServiceRequired(rateResults, shipmentRequest) // returns boolean
    function BackupServiceRequired(rateResults,shipmentRequest)
    {
        var ratedArriveDate = GetStringArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);

        var formattedArriveDate = stringToDate(ratedArriveDate, dateFormat, "-");

        var requestedDeliveryDate = stringToDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5, dateFormat, "-");

        var applyBackupService = (requestedDeliveryDate < formattedArriveDate);

        return applyBackupService;
    }

// function ApplyRulesWithServiceRequested(shipmentRequest, rateResults, dateToday) // returns void
    function ApplyRulesWithServiceRequested(shipmentRequest,rateResults,dateToday)
    {
        var requestedServiceSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
        var backupNDADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; //UPSAPI.UPS.NDA        
        var backupExpressIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS  
        var serviceToBeReturned = '';
        var domestic = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === "US";

        rateResults.slice()
                   .forEach(function(item, index, object) 
        {            
            if (!requestedServiceSymbol) 
            {
                requestedServiceSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
            }

            serviceToBeReturned = requestedServiceSymbol;

            var requestedServiceIsFoundAsRateResult = (item.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

            if (requestedServiceIsFoundAsRateResult) 
            {                                           
                console.log("Found requested service in position: " + index + "of rate results");

                var applyBackupService = BackupServiceRequired(rateResults,shipmentRequest);

                if (applyBackupService)
                {
                    if (domestic) 
                    {
                        serviceToBeReturned = backupNDADomesticService;                

                        UpdateFields(formatDate(getTomorrowDate(),true));  
                    }                
                    else
                    {
                        serviceToBeReturned = backupExpressIntlService;

                        rateResults.forEach(function(item, index, object) 
                        {
                            if (item.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === backupExpressIntlService) 
                            {
                                UpdateFields(formatDate(GetArriveDate(item.PackageDefaults.ArriveDate)),applyBackupService);                  
                            }
                        });                       
                    }
                }
                else
                {
                    if (rateResults) 
                    {
                        var fullArriveDate = GetArriveDate(rateResults[0].PackageDefaults.ArriveDate);

                        UpdateFields(fullArriveDate,false);                         
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }

// function stringToDate(_date, _format, _delimiter) // returns Date
    function stringToDate(_date, _format, _delimiter)
    {
        var formatLowerCase = _format.toLowerCase();
        var formatItems = formatLowerCase.split(_delimiter);
        var dateItems = _date.split(_delimiter);
        var monthIndex = formatItems.indexOf("mm");
        var dayIndex = formatItems.indexOf("dd");
        var yearIndex = formatItems.indexOf("yyyy");
        var month = parseInt(dateItems[monthIndex]);
        month -= 1;
        var formatedDate = new Date(dateItems[yearIndex], month, dateItems[dayIndex]);
        return formatedDate;
    }

// Source: Meta Platforms Facebook (METAPLATFORMSFACEBOOK)_Meta Return Client Rules Phase 2_1857.cs
// function isComplete(item) // returns boolean indicating whether the item passes required-field checks
        function isComplete(item) {
            var result = false;
            if (item.AssetType == '' || item.AssetType.BoxSizeId == 999)
                $('[ng-model="vm.selectedAssetType"]').focus();
            else if (item.BoxSize == '' || item.BoxSize == undefined)
                '[ng-model="vm.selectedBoxSize"]'.focus(); //wait to focus
            else if (item.AssetTagOrSerialNumber == '') {
                $('[ng-model="vm.assetTagOrSerialNumber"]').focus();
            }                
            else 
                result = true;
            return result;
        }

// function updateConsigneeStateProvince(country) // returns void
        function updateConsigneeStateProvince(country) {
            this.consigneeStateProvince = [];
            if (country == 'US') this.consigneeStateProvince = client.shipping.stateProvince.unitedStates;
            else if (country == 'CA') this.consigneeStateProvince = client.shipping.stateProvince.canada;
            this.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Phone'].IsRequired = country == 'CA';
        }

// function clearNameAddress(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) // returns void
        function clearNameAddress(shipmentRequest, nameAddress) {
            if (nameAddress == 'Consignee') {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
                    Company: this.profile.FieldOptions['Consignee.Company'].DefaultValue,
                    Email: client.userName
                }
                shipmentRequest.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = '';
            }
            client.shipping.contact.focus();
        }

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        clearAlert();
        shipmentRequest.loader = true;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = null;
        //disableConsigneeNameAddress(true);
    };

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        loadText.val('');
        shipmentRequest.loader = false;

        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1.ShowConsignee) {
            disableConsigneeNameAddress(false);
            setFocus(consigneeCompany);
        } else {
            setFocus('input[name="unitValue_txt"]'); // weight field
        }
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = null;
        //shipmentRequest.Consignee.Phone == '888-555-1212';
    };

// this.DimensionChange(packaging) // returns void
    this.DimensionChange = function (packaging) {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.packageIndex + 1; i++) {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Packaging = packaging;

            if (packaging == "LETTER") {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Height = '';
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Length = '';
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Width = '';
            }
        }

        //make sure dims are required
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Length"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Width"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Height"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";

        generalDimensionLength.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
        generalDimensionWidth.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
        generalDimensionHeight.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
    };

// this.NameAddressChange(addressName) // returns void
    this.NameAddressChange = function (addressName) {
        var nameAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'OriginAddress') nameAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress;

        nameAddress.StateProvince = nameAddress.StateProvince.toUpperCase(); //fix issue with UPS Adapter state case issue
    };

// this.DimensionChange(packaging) // returns void
    this.DimensionChange = function (packaging) {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.packageIndex + 1; i++) {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Packaging = packaging;

            if (packaging == "LETTER") {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Height = '';
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Length = '';
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Width = '';
            }
        }

        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Length"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Width"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Height"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";

        generalDimensionLength.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
        generalDimensionWidth.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
        generalDimensionHeight.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
    };

                            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
                        });

                        $('div[property="MiscReference2"]').children()[1].maxLength = 2;
                        $('div[property="MiscReference3"]').children()[1].maxLength = 8;
                        $('div[property="MiscReference4"]').children()[1].maxLength = 5;
                        $('div[property="MiscReference5"]').children()[1].maxLength = 4;
                        $('div[property="MiscReference6"]').children()[1].maxLength = 6;
                        $('div[property="MiscReference7"]').children()[1].maxLength = 10;
                        $('div[property="MiscReference8"]').children()[1].maxLength = 8;

                        //added for showing error message

                        $('div[property="MiscReference3"]').children()[1].addEventListener("focus", function() {
                            $('div[property="MiscReference3"]').children()[2].hidden = true;
                        });

                        $('div[property="MiscReference3"]').children()[1].addEventListener("blur", function() {
                            $('div[property="MiscReference3"]').children()[2].hidden = false;
                            //$('div[property="MiscReference3"]').children()[2].style.cssText = "color:red";

                        });


                    }
                }
            }, 50);

        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {

        //uncomment this to auto get weight
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        debugger;

        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }//end of this.shipping

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {

        //enable this to get weight auto at order load time
        this.vm.getWeight();
		debugger;
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        checkForCancelled(this.vm);
        sumCommodities();

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

        function checkForCancelled(view) {

            var $misc19 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]');

            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if ($misc19.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);

                        if ($misc19.val() == "T") {
                            debugger;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip = true;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisablePendingShipment = true;
                            $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            alert("This order is marked as Cancelled. Please load a new order");
                        }
                    }
                }, 50);

            }
        }
		

        function sumCommodities()
        {
            var commoditiesValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents.map(m => +m.Quantity * +m.UnitValue.Amount);
            var commTotal = 0.00;
            if(!commoditiesValue || Array.isArray(commoditiesValue ) || arr.commoditiesValue  !== 0)
            {
                for (let i = 0; i < commoditiesValue.length; i++) {
                    commTotal += commoditiesValue[i];
                  }
            }
            $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $' + commTotal);
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');

        $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

        $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', false);
    }

// Source: National Collectors Mint (NACOMI)_NCM Trial CBR_2467.cs
// loadWeight() // returns void
        function loadWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration === undefined) return;
            var scale = this.profile.ScaleConfiguration;
            var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read';
            var data = {
                'PortType': scale.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                'Port': scale.Port,
                'UsbVid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                'UsbPid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                'RequestCommand': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                'BaudRate': scale.ScaleDefinition.BaudRate,
                'StopBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                'Parity': scale.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                'DataBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.DataBits,
                'RequestTimeout': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                'HostAddress': scale.HostAddress,
                'RegexPattern': scale.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                'DeviceParser': scale.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                'DeviceName': scale.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                'Handshake': scale.ScaleDefinition.Handshake,
                'RetryCount': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryCount,
                'RetryDelay': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryDelay
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": ret.WeightUnit === null ? "LB" : ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                };


            } else {
                client.alert.Danger(this.translations.Common.ErrorCode + " : " + ret.ErrorCode + "  " + ret.ErrorMessage);
            }            
        }

// Source: NetApp, Inc (NetApp)_Netapp Reference Business Rule_61.cs
// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetShipment(shipmentRequest).UserRef1;
        ValidateReference(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.ShipperReference.FieldOptionValidations)    ;
    }

// function ValidateReference(referenceValue, referenceList) // returns void
    function ValidateReference(referenceValue, referenceList){
        var readyToShip = false;
        for(var data in referenceList){
            if(referenceList[data].Value == referenceValue){
                readyToShip = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if(readyToShip === false)throw ({message:"Unable to validate shipment",errorCode:"001"});
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        if (location === '/shipping')
        {
            var loadInterval = setInterval(function()
            {
                loadText = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
                if (loadText.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(loadInterval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]', 'keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 13 && $(this).val().indexOf(".") !== -1)
                {
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[1]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[2]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[0]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                }
            });
        }
    };

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //Setting the return address on Dicks Sporting Goods orders to their address
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 == "8778469997")
        {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Company = "Dicks Sporting Goods";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Contact = "";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address1 = "1314 Conklin Rd.";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address2 = "STE B";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.City = "Conklin";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.StateProvince = "NY";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.PostalCode = "13748";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Country = "US";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Phone = "8778469997";
        }
        
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling)
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = addressBookEntries[0].Address2;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address3 = addressBookEntries[0].Address3;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = addressBookEntries[0].City;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = addressBookEntries[0].StateProvince;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = addressBookEntries[0].PostalCode;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = addressBookEntries[0].Country;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Phone = addressBookEntries[0].Phone;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }   
        else if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms == "CONSIGNEE")
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }
        $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').focus();
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 == "RTGD")
        {
            alert("Please ensure to rate and select the desired service for shipping.");
        }
    };

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityClass = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityClass;
    };

// GetAddressBook(addressBookName, context) // returns address book object or undefined
    this.GetAddressBook = function (addressBookName, context) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false);
        if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
            client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
        } else {
            if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                client.alert.Danger('Address Book: "' + addressBookName + '" does not exist');                
            } else {
                return response.AddressBooks[0];
            }
        }
    }

// GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, context, codeReference) // returns address book entries array or undefined
    this.GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBook, context, codeReference) {
        if (addressBook != undefined) {
            var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Code", FieldValue: codeReference, Operator: 0 }] };
            var data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBook.Id], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: context.CompanyId, SiteId: context.SiteId, UserId: context.UserId };
            var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false);
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } else {
                if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                    client.alert.Danger('Address Book Entries: No address found in "' + addressBookName + '" address book');
                } else {
                    return response.AddressBookEntries;
                }
            }
        }
    }

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        if (typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 !== "undefined") 
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = "";
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// getDates(vm) // returns undefined
function getDates(vm){
	vm.getTdDates = function(shipper) {

	    var AllShipperList, selectShipper, shipperId;
	    AllShipperList=vm.profile.Shippers;

        selectShipper = AllShipperList.find(function(s) {
            return s.Symbol === shipper;
        });
        shipperId = selectShipper ? selectShipper.Id : null;
	   
	    var shipExecServiceUrl = clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
		var authorizationToken = clientService.authorizationToken();
		var getShipperCarriersmethod,getManifestItemsList,getManifestItemsemethod,methodParams,searchPackageHistorymethod,searchMethodParams;
	    
	    
		getShipperCarriersmethod='api/ShippingService/GetShipperCarriers';
		getManifestItemsemethod='api/ShippingService/GetManifestItems';
		searchPackageHistorymethod='api/ShippingService/SearchPackageHistory';
	    
	    var getShipperCarriersmethodParams = {"ShipperId":shipperId,"CompanyId":client.userContext.CompanyId};
	    var SelectedCarrier =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getShipperCarriersmethod, data: getShipperCarriersmethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;
	    var carrier = SelectedCarrier.Carriers[0].Symbol;
	    
		methodParams = {"Carrier":carrier,"Shipper":shipper,"SearchCriteria":{"OrderByClauses":[{"FieldName":"ShipDate","Direction":"DESC"}]},"IncludeImported":false,"CompanyId":client.userContext.CompanyId};
        getManifestItemsList =  $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + getManifestItemsemethod, data: methodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;

	    var totalRecords =0;
	    searchMethodParams = {"SearchCriteria":{"WhereClauses":[{"FieldName":"Shipper","FieldValue":shipper,"Operator":0},{"FieldName":"Voided","FieldValue":false,"Operator":0}]},"TotalRecords":totalRecords,"CompanyId":client.userContext.CompanyId};
        
	    var allPkgs = $.post({url: clientService.config.ApiUrl + '/' + searchPackageHistorymethod, data: searchMethodParams, async: false, headers: authorizationToken }).responseJSON;


        vm.SelectedManifestItems = vm.ManifestItems.map(function(item) {
            const pkg = allPkgs.Packages.find(p => p.ManifestName === item.Name);
            if (pkg) {
                vm.getManifestLabel = function(item) {
                    var pkg = allPkgs.Packages.find(function(p) { return p.ManifestName === item.Name; });
                    if (pkg && pkg.Shipdate) {
                        var date = pkg.Shipdate;
                        var formattedDate = date.Year + '-' + String(date.Month).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(date.Day).padStart(2, '0');
                        return item.Name + ' [' + formattedDate + ']';
                    }
                    return item.Name;
                };
            }
            return null;
        }).filter(Boolean);
	}

// this.PreSearchHistory(searchCriteria) // returns undefined
this.PreSearchHistory = function(searchCriteria) {


		if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses !== null && searchCriteria.WhereClauses !== undefined) {
			if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses.length > 0) {
				var StartShipDate = null;
				var EndShipDate = null;
				var Shipper = "";
				for (var i = 0; i <= searchCriteria.WhereClauses.length - 1; i++) {
					if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "Shipper") {
						Shipper = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldValue;
					} else if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "Shipdate" && StartShipDate == null) {
						StartShipDate = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldValue;
					} else if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "Shipdate" && StartShipDate != null) {
						EndShipDate = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldValue;
					} else if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "MiscReference1") {
						var miscReferenceObject = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i];
						searchCriteria.WhereClauses.splice(i, 1);
						searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({
							"FieldName": "ConsolidationTrackingNumber",
							"FieldValue": miscReferenceObject.FieldValue,
							"Operator": miscReferenceObject.Operator
						});
					}
				}



				var data = {
					UserContext: client.userContext,
					Data: "ShipDate=" + StartShipDate + ";" + "Shipper=" + Shipper
				}
				if (StartShipDate == EndShipDate) {
					sendSearchPackages("UserMethod", data, false)
				} else {
					var divResults = document.getElementById("divResults");
					divResults.innerHTML = "Select one day only to show package count!";
				}
			}
		}

	}

// HighlightWrongOrderNumber() // returns undefined
function HighlightWrongOrderNumber() {
		$('input[name="orderNumber"]').focusout(function() {
			$(this).css("background-color", ($(this).val().length > 0 && $(this).val().length < 8) ? "#f44336" : "#FFFFFF");
		})
	}

// Source: Novo Nordisk CA (NovonordiskCA)_NovonordiskCA Reference Rules_19.cs
// IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean
IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) {
      var isValid = false;
      if (this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
         var options = this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations;
         options.forEach(function (option) {
            if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
         });
      }

      if(referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
      return isValid;
   }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        vm = this.vm;

// ValidateCostCenterAccount() // returns boolean
    function ValidateCostCenterAccount() {
        
        var customData = vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
        
        var returnValue = true;
        if (customData.length > 0) {
          
            var costCenters = getValueByKey("CustomData1", customData)
            var accounts = getValueByKey("CustomData3", customData);
            var costCenterCount = 0;
            if(costCenters != "")
            { 
                costCenterCount =  costCenters.indexOf(",") > 0 ? costCenters.split(",").length : 1;
            }
            var accountsCount = 0;
            if(accounts != "")
            { 
                accountsCount =  accounts.indexOf(",") > 0 ? accounts.split(",").length : 1;
            }
            
            if (costCenterCount != accountsCount) {
                returnValue =  false;
            }
        }
        return returnValue
    }

// getCostCenterByShipper(selectedShipper) // returns string
    function getCostCenterByShipper(selectedShipper) {
        
        var customData = vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
       
        var shippers = getValueByKey("CustomData3", customData);
       
        var shipperData = shippers.split(",");
        var index = shipperData.indexOf(selectedShipper);
        var costCenters = getValueByKey("CustomData1", customData);
        var costCenterData = costCenters.split(",");
        var costCenter = ''
        if (costCenterData.length > 0 && costCenterData.length >= index) {
            costCenter = costCenterData[index].trim();
        }
        return costCenter;
    }

// getEmployeeId() // returns string
    function getEmployeeId() {
        var customData = vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
        var employeeId = getValueByKey("CustomData2", customData).trim();
        return employeeId;
    }

// getValueByKey(key, arr) // returns string
    function getValueByKey(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

// Source: PackVerify Demos (PACKVERIFY)_PV Sliding Panel CBR_1858.cs
// ShowAssignGoodsPane() // returns void
ShowAssignGoodsPane()
    {
      let that = this;

      //get rid of any previous entries
      $('#listItemContainer li:gt(0)').remove();

      //change the column width to make the descriptions longer
      //change this back when the user clicks the 'Apply' button
      $('div.ui-tab-container').toggleClass('col-md-8 col-md-6').siblings('div').toggleClass('col-md-4 col-md-6')

      //set a reference to the packages object as well as the commodities objects
      this.packages = this.viewModel.currentShipment.Packages;
      this.goods = this.json.data.map(m => m.boxes).flat();
      this.goods.sort((a, b) => { return a.skuId - b.skuId });

      //loop the commodities to create a master list item for each
      $(this.goods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let k = 'e' + (Math.random() + 1).toString(36).substring(2);
        b.UniqueId = k;

        //copy the source element
        let item = $('#liClone').clone(true).data(b);

        //change the id of the main containing element so we don't run into issue later
        //each clone is a discreet list item which corresponds to a commodity
        $(item).attr('id', k);

        //the customer is sending amounts that have sometimes 10 digits after the decimal point which is throwing exceptions when trying
        //to parseFloat so this is the simplest way to get around that.
        //let cost = Math.round(b.UnitValue.Amount * 100) / 100;

        $(item).find('.goods-sku').html('SKU: <strong>' + b.skuId + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-quantity').html('Quantity: <strong>' + b.quantity + '</strong>');
        $(item).find('.goods-declared-value').html('Unit Cost: <strong>$' + b.unitPrice + '</strong>');

        //append it to our list
        $('#divAssignCommodities ul.list-group').append(item);

        //assign all goods to the first package
        that.packages[0].CommodityContents.push(that.GetCommodityContentObject(b));

        //update the weight and declared value in the root of the object
        let weight = that.packages[0].Weight;
        let dva = that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount;
        const thisWeight = (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs);
        const thisValue = (+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice);

        if (!weight.Amount) { weight.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].Weight.Amount += (+b.quantity * +b.weightLbs).toFixed(2);

        if (!dva.Amount) { dva.Amount = 0; }
        that.packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += Math.round((+b.quantity * +b.unitPrice) * 100) / 100;

        //show it gracefully
        $(item).show();
      });

      //that.UpdatePackageCounts();
      //$('li[heading=Goods] a:first').click();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').show().animate({ left: 0 }, 400);
      $('.scan-input:visible').first().focus();
      $('#divAssignCommodities').find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();
    }

// GetCommodityContentObject(data) // returns cc object
GetCommodityContentObject(data)
    {
      let cc = {};
      cc.Quantity = data.quantity;
      cc.ProductCode = data.skuId;
      cc.QuantityUnitMeasure = 'EA';
      cc.UnitValue = { Currency: 'USD', Amount: +data.unitPrice };
      cc.UnitWeight = { Units: 'LB', Amount: +data.weightLbs };
      cc.UniqueId = data.UniqueId;
      cc.PkgIndex = data.PkgIndex || 1;
      cc.PVTotalWeight = (+data.quantity * +data.weightLbs);
      cc.PVTotalValue = (+data.quantity * +data.unitPrice);

      return cc;
    }

// MoveGoodToBox(li, destBox) // returns false | void
MoveGoodToBox(li, destBox)
    {
      let vm = this.ClassViewModel;
      let that = this;
      let data = $(li).data();
      let destCC = this.packages[destBox - 1].CommodityContents || [];

      //find the box the item currently resides in
      //split this statement up over a few calls to make it easier to read
      let allGoods = this.packages.map(m => m.CommodityContents).flat();
      let item = allGoods.find(cc => cc.UniqueId == data.UniqueId);

      if (+item.PkgIndex == +destBox) { console.log('Item already exists in box.'); return false; }

      //remove the item from its current box
      this.packages[item.PkgIndex - 1].CommodityContents = this.packages[item.PkgIndex - 1].CommodityContents.filter(p => p.UniqueId != data.UniqueId);

      //add it to the new box
      item.PkgIndex = destBox;
      destCC.push(item);
      $(li).find('.pkg-index-text').fadeOut().promise().done(function(e) { $(this).text(destBox).fadeIn(); });

      //console.log(vm.currentShipment.Packages);
      $('li[heading="Goods"]:visible:first > a').trigger('click');
      $('#goods .btn-group').find('.btn:gt(0)').not('.active').first().trigger('click');

      //update the weights and values
      //this data will have changed by now so get a new reference to the object
      allGoods = this.packages.map(m => m.CommodityContents).flat();
      //the items array will have the CommodityContents object for every package in the shipment

      //sort by package index
      //update the weight and declared values for all the packages in the shipment
      allGoods = allGoods.sort((a, b) => { return a.PkgIndex - b.PkgIndex });
      $(allGoods).each(function(a, b)
      {
        let pkg = that.packages[b.PkgIndex - 1];

        if ((a == 0) || (b.PkgIndex != allGoods[a - 1].PkgIndex))
        {
          pkg.Weight.Amount = 0;
          pkg.DeclaredValueAmount.Amount = 0;
        }

        pkg.Weight.Amount += +b.PVTotalWeight;
        pkg.DeclaredValueAmount.Amount += +b.PVTotalValue;
      });
    }

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
   GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      
      if (customDataType === "User")
      {
          if(this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress)
          {
            customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
          }
      }
      
      if (customDataType === "To") 
      {
          if(this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee)
          {
            customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
          }
      }
      
      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }

function ClientBusinessRules() {
  
   this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

class Shipment {
   constructor(shipmentRequest) {
      this.ShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
   }

 
   get UserEmail() { return this.GetEmail(); }

   get UserRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User"); }
   get UserRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User"); }
   get UserRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User"); }
   get UserRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "User"); }
   get UserRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "User"); }
   get UserRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "User"); }
   get UserRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "User"); }
   get UserRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "User"); }
   get UserRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "User"); }
   get UserRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "User"); }

   get ToRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "To"); }
   get ToRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "To"); }
   get ToRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "To"); }
   get ToRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "To"); }
   get ToRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "To"); }
   get ToRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "To"); }
   get ToRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "To"); }
   get ToRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "To"); }
   get ToRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "To"); }
   get ToRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "To"); }

   GetEmail(){
      var emailText = "";
      var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a"); 
      Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
         if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!","").trim(); 
      });
      return emailText;
   }
   
   GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
      if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }
// End Shipment Class    
}

// myMethod() // returns void
function myMethod() {
        if ($('#ordersPerPage').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#ordersPerPage').val("10");
        }
        if ($('#pageNumber').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#pageNumber').val("1");
        }
        if ($('#dateAfter').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#dateAfter').val("2021-01-01");
        }
        if ($('#batchType').val().trim() === "" || $('#batchType').val().search("undefined") > -1) {
            $('#batchType').val("processing");
        }
    }

    this.PreRate = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {

// this.IsValidated(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean
    this.IsValidated = function(referenceField, referenceValue) {
        var isValid = false;
        if (this.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
            var options = this.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations;
            options.forEach(function (option) {
                if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
            });
        }
        if(referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
        return isValid;
    };

// DefaultDangerousGoods() // returns void
function DefaultDangerousGoods() {
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var divHaz = $('div[class="modal-dialog modal-lg"]');

// RemovingCurrency() // returns void
function RemovingCurrency() {
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var divDecVal = $('div[value-property="DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount"]');
            if (divDecVal.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                //var div = divDecVal.find('div[class="input-group my-group"]');
                var select = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Currency"]');
                //debugger;
                select.empty();
                select.append($('<option>', {
                    label: 'CAD',
                    value: 'string:CAD',
                    text: 'CAD'
                }));
                select.append($('<option>', {
                    label: 'USD',
                    value: 'string:USD',
                    text: 'USD'
                }));
                select.prop("selectedIndex", 1);
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// HidingDefaultShipDate() // returns void
function HidingDefaultShipDate () {
        var date = new Date();
        var dateStr = date.getFullYear() + "-" + ("00" + (date.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2) + "-" + ("00" + date.getDate()).slice(-2);
        //debugger;
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var input = $('input[datepicker-options="vm.shipDateOptions"]');
            if (input.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                input.value(dateStr);
            }
        }, 50);
        
        
        
    }

                                '<div class="form-check" property="ProofRequireSignature" model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ProofRequireSignature" caption="Require Proof of Delivery Signature"><input type="checkbox" class="form-check-input ng-pristine ng-valid ng-empty ng-touched" ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ProofRequireSignature"><label class="form-check-label ng-binding" style="padding-left: 6px;">Require Proof of Delivery Signature</label></div>';

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
		// This function is called only when Shipment Mode = Together (option 0)
		//debugger;
		// Copy some previous package settings to new one
		// if ($('select[ng-model="vm.shipMode"]').find('option:selected').val() === "number:0")
		// {
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].UserData1;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].ShipperReference;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].ConsigneeReference;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference2;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference3;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference4;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference5;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].Description;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommercialInvoiceMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].CommercialInvoiceMethod;
			shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SaturdayDelivery = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].SaturdayDelivery;
		//}

		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
	};

// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === undefined) {
			alert("No service selected!");
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null  && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage === 'validate')
		{
			// click validate button
			$('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('button[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').click();
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(0, 4) === 'pop:') {
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== '')
		{
			alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}
		
		//getWeight(this.vm);   // TODO: disabled until scale issue resolved
		
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship')
		{
			if (!this.vm.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip) {
				this.vm.checkShip();
			}
		}
	};

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== 0)
		{
			alert("Shipping error: " + shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode);
		}
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = false;    // signature_required_checkbox
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = true;    // autoship_checkbox
	};

// thirdPartyBillingDisabled(isDisabled) // returns undefined
function thirdPartyBillingDisabled(isDisabled) {
            var $tpb = $('div[property="ThirdPartyBilling"]');
            if (isDisabled) {
                this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = false;
                this.thirdPartyBilling();
                $tpb.find('input').attr('disabled', true);
                $tpb.find('label').addClass('disabled');
            } else {
                $tpb.find('input').removeAttr('disabled');
                $tpb.find('label').removeClass('disabled');
            }
        }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {  
        //validate comment required
        var ServiceChangeCode = $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"] :input').val();
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol != shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10){
            if(ServiceChangeCode == "string:Other - Comment Field" && (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12 == null || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12 == "")){
                throw new Error('WARNING: Service Change Comment is required');
            } else if(ServiceChangeCode == "string:-- choose option --" || ServiceChangeCode == "?" || ServiceChangeCode == "" || ServiceChangeCode == null) {
                throw new Error('WARNING: Service Change Reason Code is required');
            }
        } else {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11 = "Select Option";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12 = "";
        }

        // weight package rule
        for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            if(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount == null | shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount == ""){
                var pagckageNum = i+1;
                throw new Error('WARNING: Package '+pagckageNum+' is missing a weight value');
            }
        }

        // 150lb package rule
        for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            if(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount > 150){
                var pagckageNum = i+1;
                throw new Error('WARNING: Package '+pagckageNum+' Has a weight of more than 150Lbs');
            }
        }

        // ShipDate in the past
        var now = new Date();
        var Year = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year;
        var Month = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month - 1;
        var Day = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day;
        var shipDate = new Date(Year, Month, Day);
        if(shipDate.setHours(0,0,0,0) < now.setHours(0,0,0,0)){
            throw new Error('WARNING: Package ShipDate is in the past');
        }
        
        // Weight units is not LB
        for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            if(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Units != 'LB'){
                var pagckageNum = i+1;
                throw new Error('WARNING: Package '+pagckageNum+' Has an incorrect unit for weight. Please use LB');
            }
        }
    }

// Source: SAVERS (SAVERS)_Savers Client Side Rules_1715.cs
// setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries) // returns void
    function setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries)
    {
        var countryStringValue = ('string:' + selectedCountries.join('|string:')).split('|');
        var interval = setInterval(function()

        {
            var consigneeCountries = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"] option');
            if (consigneeCountries.length)
            {
                clearInterval(interval);
                Array.from(consigneeCountries).forEach(function(opt)

                {
                    if (opt.value != '')
                    {
                        if (!countryStringValue.includes(opt.value))
                        {
                            opt.remove();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }, 50);            
    }

// setCurrencyOptions(list, element) // returns void
function setCurrencyOptions(list, element)
    {
        var interval = setInterval(function() 
            {
                var currencies = $(element);
                if (currencies.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function(){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
    }

// replaceOptionValues(list, element) // returns void
 function replaceOptionValues(list, element) {
        var valuelist = list.map(function (e) { return 'string:' + e });
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var $element = $(element);
            if ($element.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);
                $element.each(function () {
                    if (!valuelist.includes(this.value) && this.value != '') this.remove();
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns void
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns void
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        //debugger;
        var shipperSymbol = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper;

        //Skip Ship Goods Type Selection for these international shipper origins
        if (shipperSymbol != "SEGONZAC_FR" && shipperSymbol != "SURREY_UK" && shipperSymbol != "DUBLIN_IE" && shipperSymbol != "NAYANDA_IN" && shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            var shipGoodsType = document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').options[document.getElementById('ship_goods_type').selectedIndex].value;
            var pkg1MiscRef4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
            //if (shipGoodsType == null || shipGoodsType == 'undefined' || shipGoodsType == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default')
            if (pkg1MiscRef4 == null || pkg1MiscRef4 == undefined || pkg1MiscRef4 == '' || shipGoodsType == 'default') {
                $("#ship_goods_type").val('default');
                //$('#ship_goods_type').css('background-color', '#FF3333');
                $('#ship_goods_type').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Shipment Goods Type on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
                return;
            }
        }

        //#region Require Field Validation
        if (shipperSymbol != "FRANKFORT_RETURNS") {
            //debugger;
            //var costCodeValue = $("#ctl00_cphContent_right_tabs_ref_tab_ref_ctrl_misc_ref_pane_content_misc_reference_3_txt").val();
            var costCodeValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
            if (costCodeValue == null || costCodeValue == undefined || costCodeValue == '') {
                $('#costcodes').focus();
                var errorMessage = "Error, You must select a Cost Code value on the first package of the shipment";
                alert(errorMessage);
            }
        }
        //#endregion

        var thirdParty = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference19;
        var adultSignature = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].MiscReference20;

        userParams.third_party_rule = thirdParty;
        userParams.adult_signature_required_rule = adultSignature;
    };

// consigneeAddress() // returns array of address book entries
var consigneeAddress = function () {
       
        var userContext = client.userContext; 
        var shipper =  $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val();
        if(shipper != ''){
         shipper = shipper.replace('string:', '');
        }
        else{
         shipper = 'SCH_FARGO';
        }
            
        var address =  GetAddressBookEntries('Return', userContext, shipper);
        return address;
    }

// thirdPartyBillingAddress() // returns array of address book entries
var thirdPartyBillingAddress = function () {
        var userContext = client.userContext; 
        var shipper = 'SCH_FARGO';
        var address =  GetAddressBookEntries('Return', userContext, shipper);
        return address;
    }

// GetAddressBookEntries(addressBookName, context, shipper) // returns address book entries or throws on missing data
var GetAddressBookEntries = function (addressBookName, context, shipper) {
        var searchCriteria = { WhereClauses: [{ FieldName: "Name", FieldValue: addressBookName, Operator: 0 }] };
        var data = { CompanyId: context.CompanyId, UserId: context.UserId };
        var response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
            throw ({ message: 'Address Book:"' + addressBookName + '" does not exists'});
        } else {
            var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
            
            searchCriteria = { Skip: 0, WhereClauses: [{FieldName: "Code", FieldValue: shipper, Operator: 0}], OrderByClauses: [] };
            data = { AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, UserContext :{Machine:""} , CompanyId: context.CompanyId, UserId: context.UserId };
            response = thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries', data, false).responseJSON;
            
            if (response.TotalRecords == 0) {
                throw ({ message: 'Address Book:"' + addressBookName + '" does not have any address entry'});
            } else {
                return response.AddressBookEntries;
            }
        }
    }

// Source: Schenker, Inc (schenker)_Schenker CBR 2.3 Fix_1756.cs
// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // throws if ShipperReference is invalid
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        var shipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: "Cost Center is invalid [" + shipperReference + "].", errorCode: "001" });
        }
    };

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void; defaults ShipperReference and validates it
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.IsValid = this.IsValidated;
        var originCustomData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('Custom1', originCustomData);

        if (!this.vm.IsValid('ShipperReference', shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference)) {
            throw ({ message: 'Cost Center is invalid from User Custom Data', errorCode: '001' });
        }

        if (pageLoaded) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired
            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
        }
    };

// this.IsValidated(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean
    this.IsValidated = function (referenceField, referenceValue) {
        var isValid = false;
        if (this.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
            var options = this.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations;
            options.forEach(function (option) {
                if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
            });
        }
        //if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
        return isValid;
    };

// function setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement() // returns void; adjusts required fields and UI state
    function setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement() {
        var isRequired = vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'US';
        if (!isRequired) {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = false;

            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = descriptionIsRequired;
            descriptionLabel.css('color', '#337ab7');

            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = consigneePhoneIsRequired;
            consigneePhoneLabel.css('color', '#337ab7');
            consigneePhone.css('border-color', 'rgb(169,68,66)');

        } else {
            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.StateProvince"].IsRequired = consigneeStateIsRequired;

            vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = false;
            descriptionLabel.css('color', '#333333');

            vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = false;
            consigneePhoneLabel.css('color', '#333333');
            consigneePhone.css('border-color', 'rgb(204,204,204)');

        }
    }

// function documentReady() // returns void; sets default required states and hooks validation-triggering change handler
    function documentReady() {
        vm.fieldOptions.Description.IsRequired = false;
        descriptionLabel.css('color', '#333333');

        vm.fieldOptions["Consignee.Phone"].IsRequired = false;
        consigneePhoneLabel.css('color', '#333333');
        consigneePhone.css('border-color', 'rgb(204,204,204)')

        consigneeCountry.change(function (e) {
            setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement();
        });

    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
