// GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
    function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

// Source: Soundoff Signal (SOS)_Warehouse Shipping CBR_1803.cs
// TableRowDataObject(RowId) // returns the matching table-row data object or undefined
  TableRowDataObject = (RowId) =>
  {
    return this.#AllTableRowDataObjects.filter(r => r.RowId == RowId)[0];
  }

// TableRowPackedItemCount(RowId, ContainerIndex) // returns the packed item count for the row/container, total row quantity, or null
  TableRowPackedItemCount = (RowId, ContainerIndex) =>
  {
    const data = this.#PackedItemDataObjects.filter(r => r.RowId == RowId)[0];

    //if there are no packed items in the passed row, return
    if (!data) return null;

    if (RowId && ContainerIndex)
    {
      //return the count of the items in the passed container index
      const r = data.PackedItems.filter(d => d.ContainerIndex == ContainerIndex);
      return (r.length > 0 ? r[0].Count : 0);
    }
    else
    {
      //return the total count of all packed items for this row in ALL containers
      //don't need to calculate this value as it's part of the root data object
      return this.TableRowDataObject(RowId).QuantityPacked;
    }
  }

// GetContainersForFocusedItem(RowId) // returns an array of container indexes or undefined
  GetContainersForFocusedItem = (RowId) =>
  {
    const data = this.#AllListItemDataObjects;
    const rows = data.filter(d => d.RowId == RowId)[0];

    //only need the 0 index because the first entry will have the entire container list with it
    if (rows && rows.PackedItems)
    {
      return rows.PackedItems.map(m => m.ContainerIndex);
    }
    return undefined;
  }

// GetContainersHavingItem(RowId) // returns the packed-items array or undefined
  GetContainersHavingItem = (RowId) =>
  {
    const data = this.#AllListItemDataObjects;
    const row = data.filter(d => d.RowId == RowId)[0];

    if (row && row.PackedItems)
    {
      return row.PackedItems;
    }
    return undefined;
  }

// TrimAllKeysAndValues(obj) // returns the trimmed object
  TrimAllKeysAndValues = (obj) =>
  {
    for (var k in obj)
    {
      if (typeof obj[k] == "object" && obj[k] !== null)
      {
        this.TrimAllKeysAndValues(obj[k]);
      }
      else if (obj.hasOwnProperty(k))
      {
        obj[k] = (typeof obj[k] == 'string' ? obj[k].trim() : obj[k]);
      }
    }
    return obj;
  }

// InitMultipleOperationsDialog() // returns void
  InitMultipleOperationsDialog = () =>
  {
    console.log('Initializing event handlers for Multiple Operations Dialog.');

    //setup the event handlers
    let that = this;

    //event handler for selecting a container
    let ul = $('#ulMultipleItemContainerDropdown');
    $(ul).delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.stopImmediatePropagation();

      $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).find('span.ci').first().text($(this).text());
      $('ul.dropdown-menu:visible').slideUp(250);
      $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).find('span.max-value').first().text($(this).attr('data-max'));

      $('#textQuantityToMove').attr('max', $(this).attr('data-max')).removeAttr('disabled').focus();
    });

    //when the cursor leaves the QuantityToMove input box, check to make sure it has a valid value
    $('#textQuantityToMove').on('focusout', function(e)
    {
      const i = +$(this).val();
      const m = +$(this).attr('max');

      $('#btnOkMultipleOperations').attr('disabled', (i > m));

      if (i > m)
      {
        $(this).addClass('has-error');
        $(this).focus();
        $(this).tooltip('show');
        return;
      }

      $(this).removeClass('has-error');
    });

    //clicking on the dialog buttons
    $(this.multipleOperationsDialog).find('button[op]').on('click', function(e)
    {
      const op = $(this).attr('op');

      switch (op)
      {
        case 'ok':
          let [rowid, qty, ci, action] = [$(this).data('RowId'), +$('#textQuantityToMove').val(), $('span.ci').first().text(), $(this).data('Action')];
          let row = that.packVerify.DataStore.TableRowDataObject(rowid);

          switch (action)
          {
            case 'add':
              that.packVerify.AddItemDataToContainer(row, qty, ci);
              break;
            case 'remove':
              that.packVerify.RemoveItemDataFromContainer(rowid, qty, ci);
              break;
          }
          break;

        case 'cancel':
          break;

        default:
          break;
      }

      that.bRemove = false;

      if (that.packVerify.Items.Ordered !== that.packVerify.Items.Packed) that.packVerify.Overlay.Hide();
      $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).fadeOut().find('input').val([]).find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip('destroy');
      $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).find('span.footer-max').first().fadeOut();
    });

    //fired when the user selects an item from the add/remove multiple items autocomplete dialog
    //need to filter out from the container dropdown here so when a user is removing items, they don't have the option
    //to remove from a container that doesn't have the item
    $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).delegate('[event="SelectItemDropdown"]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.stopImmediatePropagation();

      const data = $(this).data();
      let maxValue = 0;

      if (that.bRemove)
      {
        const list = that.packVerify.DataStore.GetContainersHavingItem(data.RowId);
        let ul = $('#ulMultipleItemContainerDropdown'), li = '<li><a href="#"></a></li>';

        $(list).each(function(a, b)
        {
          let tt = `data-max="${b.Count}" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Maximum: ${b.Count}" data-container="body" data-html="true"`;
          li += `<li ${tt}><a href="#">${b.ContainerIndex}</a></li>`;
        });

        $('#btnContainerDropDown').removeAttr('disabled');

        $(ul).empty().append(li);

        if (list.length == 1)
        {
          //if there's only a single container, set the variable
          $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).find('span.ci').first().text(list[0].ContainerIndex);
          maxValue = list[0].Count;
        }

        $(ul).find('[data-toggle="tooltip"]').tooltip();
      }

      //store the row information with the button data object so when the user clicks 'ok', the data can be read and processed
      $('#btnOkMultipleOperations').data(data);
      $('input[event="ShowMatchingItems"]').val(data.ItemNumber);

      //change the strings depending on whether adding/removing
      let header = (that.bRemove ? 'remove.' : 'add.');
      let max = (that.bRemove ? maxValue : data.QuantityRemaining);

      $('#btnOkMultipleOperations').data('Action', header.slice(0, -1));

      $('#textQuantityToMove').attr({ 'max': max });
      $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).find('span.max-value').first().text(max);
      $(that.multipleOperationsDialog).find('span.footer-max').first().fadeIn();

      $('#ulItemAutoComplete').find('li').slideUp(250).closest('div').hide().promise().done(function(t)
      {
        if (that.bRemove)
        {
          $('#btnContainerDropDown').focus();
          if ($('#ulMultipleItemContainerDropdown').find('li').length > 2) { $('#ulMultipleItemContainerDropdown').slideDown(); }
        }
        else
        {
          $('#textQuantityToMove').focus();
        }
      });

      if ($(e.target).hasClass('all-avail')) { $('#textQuantityToMove').val(max); $('#btnContainerDropDown').focus(); }
    });

    $('[event="ShowMatchingItems"]').on('keyup search', function(e)
    {
      const ul = $('#ulItemAutoComplete');
      const [val, items, bVisible] = [$(this).val(), $(ul).find('li:visible'), $(ul).find('li:visible').length > 0];

      //need to deal with a few different scenarios
      //did the user backspace and now there are <= 2 chars?  if so, slide up all the visible list items and then remove them.  then return out after updating the tooltip.
      if (val.length < 1)
      {
        if (bVisible) $(ul).find('li').slideUp(200).promise().done((e) => { $(e).remove(); });

        //hide the menu container
        $('#divItemAutoComplete').fadeOut('fast');

        //update the tooltip
        //$('span.tooltip-search.tooltip-results').text('enter at least 3 letters');
        return;
      }

      //the menu is already visible. check the entries that are visible to see if they match the search pattern
      //then need to run the query again as we won't know if the user backspaced or edited the middle of the string
      if (bVisible)
      {
        //get rid of list items that no longer match after the text was changed.  make sure the return stays outside the .slide
        const listitems = $(items).filter((a, b) => $(b).text().toLocaleUpperCase().indexOf(val.toLocaleUpperCase()) === -1);
        $(listitems).slideUp(200).promise().done((e) => { $(e).remove(); that.ShowAutoComplete(val); });
      }
      else
      {
        //user cleared the box or clicked the 'x'
        $(ul).empty();
        that.ShowAutoComplete(val);
      }
    });
  }

// escapeString(str) // returns a sanitized string
  escapeString = (str) => { return (str + '').replace(/[\\"']/g, '').replace(/\u0000/g, '\\0'); }

// GetAutoCompleteItem(obj, val) // returns a jQuery list-item element
  GetAutoCompleteItem = (obj, val) =>
  {
    let title = this.escapeString(obj.ItemDescription);

    let div = `<div><p>${title}</p><div><span>Ordered: ${obj.QuantityOrdered}</span><span class='span-10L'>Packed: ${obj.QuantityPacked}</span></div>`;

    let li = $(`<li style="display: none;" event="SelectItemDropdown" class="menu-item" data-container="body" row-id="${obj.RowId}" data-html="true" data-toggle="tooltip" title="${div}"><a href="#"><span>${obj.ItemNumber}</span><span class="all-avail">All</span></a></li>`).data(obj);
    return li;
  }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	        	return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

    function DrawDataInReturnForm(){
        var carrierEmailReturnLabelMethod = 5;
        $('form[name="returnForm"]').find('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val(RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION);

// MarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
    function MarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = true;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 4;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = shipmentRequestObject.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = RETURN_DEFAULT_DESCRIPTION;             
        }
    }

// UnMarkShipmentAsReturn() // returns void
    function UnMarkShipmentAsReturn(){
        for (let i = 0; i < vm.currentShipment.Packages.length; i++) 
        {
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDelivery = false;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryMethod = undefined;
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = '';
             vm.currentShipment.Packages[i].Description = '';
        }
    }

// ClearAllInputFields() // returns void
    function ClearAllInputFields()
    {
        var loadedOrderValue = $('input[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();
        var elements = document.getElementsByTagName("input");        
        for (var ii=0; ii < elements.length; ii++) 
        {
            if (elements[ii].type == "text" && elements[ii].value != loadedOrderValue) 
            {
                elements[ii].value = "";
            }
        }  
        
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').prop("checked", false);
        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]>option:eq(0)').prop('selected', true)
        $('textarea[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Description"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail"]').val();
        $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmailLocale"]').val();
         shipmentRequestObject =  {}
    }

          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5 = locationCode;
    }

// Source: Sun Communities (SUNCOMMUNITIES)_SUN_Business Rules Kiosk_1600.cs
// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        var originCustomData = GetCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData) + "-" + GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData) + "," + GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);        
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = GetKeyValue('TMID', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = GetKeyValue('ENTITY', originCustomData);        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = GetKeyValue('GL_CODE', originCustomData);                
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = GetKeyValue('DEPARTMENT', originCustomData);
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Code = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        var location = GetKeyValue('LOCATION', originCustomData);
        
        // MOS or MOO to switch shipper to main office 
        if(location == "MOS" || location == "MOO")
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "MOS";
    };

// function GetCustomData(nameAddress) // returns array
    function GetCustomData(nameAddress) {
        if (nameAddress && nameAddress.CustomData) {
            return nameAddress.CustomData;
        }
        return [];
    }

// function GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
    function GetKeyValue(key, arr) {
        for (var index in arr) {
            if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
        }
        return '';
    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {

    };

// Source: Sysco Foods (SYSCO)_Client Side Business Rules 20240808_2450.cs
// customGetWeight() // returns undefined
function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                    vm.checkShip();                    
                }
            }
        }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities) // returns boolean
function ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities)
    {
        var rexVal = /^[A-Z0-9]+((,|-)[A-Z0-9]+)*[A-Z0-9]+$/;
        var result = true;
        if (!rexVal.test(consolidatedOpportunities.toUpperCase()))
        {
            if (consolidatedOpportunities.trim()==="")
            {
                result=true;
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Consolidated opportunities not well formed.");
                result= false;
            }
        }
        return result;
    }

// CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping, ConsolidatedOpportunities, OpportunityLoaded) // returns string
function CreateShippingSession(IsConsolidatedShipping,ConsolidatedOpportunities,OpportunityLoaded)
    {
        var jsonObject = {};
        jsonObject["IsConsolidatedShipping"] = IsConsolidatedShipping;
        jsonObject["ConsolidatedOpportunities"] = ConsolidatedOpportunities.split(',');
        jsonObject["OpportunityLoaded"] = OpportunityLoaded;
        return JSON.stringify(jsonObject);
    }

// Source: Target (TARGET)_Target CBR_2489.cs
// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined; may throw a ValidationError
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
        if (!shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 || shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1.trim() === '') {
            // Highlight the field if it has no value
            waitForInputs();    

            const err = new Error('MiscReference1 is required');
            err.name = 'ValidationError'; // Optional custom name
            err.code = 'MISC_REF_001';    // Custom property
            throw err;
        } else {
            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model*="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                    input.style.border = null;
                });
            }
        }

        function waitForInputs() {
            const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('[ng-model$="MiscReference1"]');
            if (inputs.length > 0) {
                inputs.forEach(input => {
                input.style.border = '1px solid red';
                });
                observer.disconnect(); // stop watchin
            }
            });

            observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });

        }
    }

                    });

// function GetDateTimeToString() // returns formatted date-time string
      function GetDateTimeToString()
        {
            var date_ = new Date();
            var year = date_.getFullYear();
            var month = date_.getMonth()+1;
            var day = date_.getDate();
            if(month<10) month = "0"+month;
            if(day<10) day = "0"+day;

            var hours = date_.getHours();
            var mins = date_.getMinutes();
            var secs = date_.getSeconds();
            var msecs = date_.getMilliseconds();
            if(hours<10) hours = "0"+hours;
            if(mins<10) mins = "0"+mins;
            if(secs<10) secs = "0"+secs;
            if(msecs<10) secs = "0"+msecs;
            return year+month+day+hours+mins+secs;
        }

// function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams){
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4
            , this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference4.FieldOptionValidations);
        CheckValidation(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5,
            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference5.FieldOptionValidations);

            this.vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference6.FieldOptionValidations);
        
    }

// CheckValidation(checkValue, checkField) // returns checkValue or throws an error
    function CheckValidation(checkValue, checkField){
        
        for(var item in checkField){
            if(checkField[item].Value == checkValue)return checkValue;
        }
        throw ({message:"Validation Error!\nUnable to ship!",errorCode:"001"});
    }

// UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns undefined
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;

        if (stateProvince == 'PR') {
            nameAddress.Country = 'PR';
        }
        else {
            nameAddress.Country = 'US';
        }
    }

// documentReady() // returns void
function documentReady() {
        $terms.add($termsOfSale).find("option:gt(0)").each(function (x, y) {
            if (y.value === 'string:CONSIGNEE') {
                y.label = 'Receiver';
            } else if (y.value == 'string:SHIPPER' || y.value === 'string:DDP') {
                y.label = 'UPS Account';
            } else {
                $(this).remove();
            }
        });

        consigneeCountry.change(function(e){
            setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement();
        });

        returnLabel.click(function(e) {
            var returnDelivery = vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery;
            var isReturn = returnDelivery == undefined || returnDelivery == true;
            returnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
        })

        returnOption.change(function(e) {
            returnNameAddressCaption(this.checked);
        })

        miscReference8.change(function(e) {
            var ref8 = $(this).val();
            if (/\d+/i.test(ref8)) {
                if (!/\d+kgs/i.test(ref8)) {
                    var match = ref8.match(/^[\d.]+/);
                    $(this).val(match[0] + "kgs").change()
                }
            }
        })

    }

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
        GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
            var returnValue = "";
            var customData = null;
            if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
            if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

            if (customData) {
                customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                    if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
                })
            }
            return returnValue;
        }

// IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean
        IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) {
            var isValid = false;
            if (this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
                var options = this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations
                options.forEach(function (option) {
                    if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
                });
            }

            if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
            return isValid;
        }

                    state = "VA";
                    break;
                case "washington":
                    state = "WA";
                    break;
                case "west virginia":
                    state = "WV";
                    break;
                case "wisconsin":
                    state = "WI";
                    break;
                case "wyoming":
                    state = "WY";
                    break;
                default:
                    alert("Please use a two character state abbreviation for US states.");
                }
            }
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince = state;
        }
        else {
            // skip validation for international
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.IsValidated = true;
        }
        var userId = userContext.UserId;
        var shipperRefence = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        var consigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
        var miscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference19 = userId;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ShipperReference = shipperReference;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[i].ConsigneeReference = consigneeReference;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference3 = miscReference3;
        }
    }

// function GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) // returns string
this.GetCustom = function(fieldName, customDataType, shipmentRequest) {
        var returnValue = "";
        var customData = null;
        if (customDataType === "User") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
        }
        if (customDataType === "To") {
            if (shipmentRequest &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee &&
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData)
                customData = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;
        }

        if (customData) {
            customData.forEach(function(customField) {
                if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
            });
        }
        return returnValue;

    };

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         vm = this.vm;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User", shipmentRequest);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User", shipmentRequest);
    };

// GetEmail() // returns string
        GetEmail() {
            var emailText = "";
            var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            Array.from(tags).forEach(function (tag) {
                if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
            });
            return emailText;
        }

// GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) // returns string
    GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
      var returnValue = "";
      var customData = null;
      if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
      if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

      if (customData) {
         customData.forEach(function (customField) {
            if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
         })
      }
      return returnValue;
   }

// IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) // returns boolean
        IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) {
            var isValid = false;
            if (this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
                var options = this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations
                options.forEach(function (option) {
                    if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
                });
            }

            if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
            return isValid;
        }

// function UserMethod(logoNumber) // returns void
function UserMethod(logoNumber) {

		if (logoNumber == 4) {

			var orderNumber = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').val();

			if (orderNumber === undefined || orderNumber === null || orderNumber === "") {

				client.alert.Danger("Missing or invalid Order Number, no update made.  Please enter a valid order number and try again.");
			}
			else {
			
				var usermethodParams = { "action": 4, "orderNumber": orderNumber, "percentageComplete":"0", "trailerNumber":"", "shipper":""};
				var results;
				var data = { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) };
				var response = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
					if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
						client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
					} else {
						results = response["Data"];
					}
				});
				
				
				/*$.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
                    async: false,
                    cache: false,
                    dataType: "json",
                    data: { UserContext: userContext, "Data": JSON.stringify(usermethodParams) },
                    success: function(response) {
                        results = response["Data"];
                        ;
                    },
                    error: function (error) {
                        alert("Finalize Shipment has failed, no update made to the system.  Contact Support.");
                    }
                });*/
			}
		}
		else {

			$("#fileLoader").click();

			var encodedBase64Logo;

			var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader").files;

			if (filesSelected.length > 0) {
				var fileToLoad = filesSelected[0];

				var fileReader = new FileReader();

				fileReader.readAsDataURL(fileToLoad);

				fileReader.onload = function (event) {
					var encodedBase64Logo = logoNumber + event.target.result;

					SoxOnWcfDblHop.userMethod(encodedBase64Logo,
						function (result) {
							// Do something with the data

							DisplayLogoSaveMessage(result);

						},
						function (e) {
							// Do something with the error

							alert(e.message);
						});
				};
			}
		}
	}

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined; throws if required field is missing
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    var consigneeCode = $('select[ng-model="xConsigneeCode"]');
    var selectCode = consigneeCode.val().substring(7);

    if (selectCode === '')
    {
      throw ({ message: 'Please select a lab', errorCode: 43770 });
    }
    var arr = this.vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes;
    var obj = arr.filter(function(nameaddress)
    {
      if (nameaddress.Code === selectCode) { return nameaddress; }
    });

    if (obj.length)
    {
      var nameaddress = obj[0];
      var consignee = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
      consignee.Company = nameaddress.Company;
      consignee.Contact = nameaddress.Contact;
      consignee.Address1 = nameaddress.Address1;
      consignee.Address2 = nameaddress.Address2;
      consignee.Address3 = nameaddress.Address3;
      consignee.City = nameaddress.City;
      consignee.StateProvince = nameaddress.StateProvince;
      consignee.PostalCode = nameaddress.PostalCode;
      consignee.Country = nameaddress.Country;
      consignee.Phone = nameaddress.Phone;
      consignee.Email = nameaddress.Email;
      consignee.Account = nameaddress.Account;

      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = GetKeyValue('shipper', nameaddress.CustomData);
      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince.toUpperCase();
    }
  };

// function ValidateShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined; throws on invalid shipment
    this.ValidateShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
    if(shipmentRequest.Packages.length>20)
    { 
        throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship more than 20 packages."};
    }
    var weight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight;
    var weightLimit = 0;
    var totalWeight = 0;
    if(weight.Units==="LB"){
            weightLimit = 150;
    }else{
        weightLimit = 68;
    }
    var i;
    for(i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++)
    {
        var pkgWeight = parseFloat(shipmentRequest.Packages[i].Weight.Amount);
       totalWeight += pkgWeight;
    }
    if(totalWeight > weightLimit){
        throw {errorCode:999,message:"You cannot ship greater than " + weightLimit + " " + weight.Units + ".  Total Weight: "+ totalWeight + " " + weight.Units};
    }
}

// function ChangeWeightUnit(e) // returns undefined
    function ChangeWeightUnit(e) {
       var country = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val();
       switch(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country)
       {
            case "US": case "GU": case "MP": case "AS": case "VI": case "PR": case "LR": case "MM":
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="LB"]').attr('selected','selected');
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="KG"]').removeAttr('selected');
                break;
            default:
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="KG"]').attr('selected','selected');
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="LB"]').removeAttr('selected');
       }


    }

// Source: WOODLAND MFG (WLMI)_WoodLand_CBR_1644.cs
// function validateOrderValue(val) // returns "VALIDAPI", "MANUAL", or "EMPTY"
    function validateOrderValue(val) {
        if ((isEmpty(val)) === false) {
            var apicallpattern = /^(61|42|57)\d{8}(\-\d{1,2})?$/;   // Actual WOODLAND
            if (apicallpattern.test(val) === true) {
                return "VALIDAPI";
            }
            else { return "MANUAL"; }
            }   
            else { return "EMPTY"; }
    }

// function isEmpty(str) // returns boolean
    function isEmpty(str) {
        return (!str || 0 === str.length);
    }

// function sbrMessage(shipment) // returns boolean
    function sbrMessage(shipment) {
        return (shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode === undefined || shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode === 0)
        && (shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== undefined && shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== 'No error' && shipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage !== null);
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.buildShipment = this.BuildShipment;
        this.vm.getUserContext = this.GetUserContext;
        this.vm.postalCodeLookup = this.PostalCodeLookup;
        this.vm.thinClientAPIRequest = this.ThinClientAPIRequest;
        this.vm.createShipmentAutoSubmit = this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit;

        shipmentRequest.selectAddress = this.SelectAddress;
        shipmentRequest.updateNameAddressCSZ = this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = this.vm.profile.Shippers[0].Symbol;

        client.shipping.consigneeCompanyFocus();

// this.BuildShipment(ret) // returns undefined
    this.BuildShipment = function (ret) {
        client.shipping.buildShipmentModalHide();

        var weightPerPackage;
        var multiPackage = this.currentShipment.Packages.length > 1;

        if (ret.TotalWeight !== undefined && ret.TotalWeight !== 0 && ret.TotalWeight !== "")
            weightPerPackage = (ret.TotalWeight / ret.TotalPackages).toFixed(3);

        for (var i = 0; i < ret.TotalPackages; i++) {
            this.packageIndex = this.currentShipment.Packages.length - 1;
            if (i > 0 || multiPackage) {
                this.addPackage();
                multiPackage = true;
            }

            if (weightPerPackage !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Amount = weightPerPackage;
            if (ret.WeightUnit !== undefined)
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = ret.WeightUnit;
            else
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight.Units = this.translations.WeightUnit;
        }
        this.totalPackages = this.currentShipment.Packages.length;

        ret.TotalWeight = '';
        ret.TotalPackages = '';
    }

// this.PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns undefined
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
debugger;
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));        
            if (responseData == null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns undefined
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress == undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;
    }

// this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns undefined
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

// this.GetUserContext(vm) // returns user context object or undefined
    this.GetUserContext = function (vm) {
        if (vm.userContext) return vm.userContext;
        if (vm.UserInformation) return vm.UserInformation;
    }

// Source: Xing Hung (XINGHUNG)_ClinetSideBussRules_1587.cs
// function BuildShipment(ret) // returns undefined
    this.BuildShipment = function (ret) {
        $buildShipmentModal.modal('hide');

        var weightPerPackage;
        var multiPackage = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length > 1;

        if (ret.TotalWeight !== undefined && ret.TotalWeight !== 0 && ret.TotalWeight !== "")
            weightPerPackage = (ret.TotalWeight / ret.TotalPackages).toFixed(3);

        for (var i = 0; i < ret.TotalPackages; i++) {
            vm.packageIndex = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length - 1;
            if (i > 0 || multiPackage) {
                vm.addPackage();
                multiPackage = true;
            }

            if (weightPerPackage !== undefined)
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount = weightPerPackage;
            if (ret.WeightUnit !== undefined)
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units = ret.WeightUnit;
            else
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units = vm.translations.WeightUnit;
        }

        vm.totalPackages = vm.currentShipment.Packages.length;

        ret.TotalWeight = '';
        ret.TotalPackages = '';
    }

// function CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns undefined
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {
            event.preventDefault();

            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($('#buildShipmentModalBody input'))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($('#buildShipmentModalBody input'))) {
                    // all shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }
    }

// Source: Zyno Medical (ZYNO)_ClientBusinessRules_1667.cs
// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        // default phone number
        if (nameaddress.Phone === '' || nameaddress.Phone === null){
            // default phone number to the return return address
            nameaddress.Phone = '(508) 650-2008';
        }

        if(nameaddress.Email !== null){
            var userEmail = nameaddress.Email;
            var senderName = 'Zyno Medical';
            
            // general visibility
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CarrierMonitoring= true;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].PriorDeliveryNotificationConsignee = true;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].NotificationFailureAddressEmail = userEmail;

            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Shipment Notification";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipNotificationDescription = '';
            
            // delivery notification
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Delivery Notification"
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryNotificationDescription = '';
            
            // delivery exeption notification
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Delivery Exeption Notification";
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].DeliveryExceptionNotificationDescription = '';
            
            // return delivery notification
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationSenderName = senderName;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationSubjectText = "ShipExec Return Delivery Notification"
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = userEmail;
            //shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryNotificationDescription = '';
           
            // remove the email field from the consignee
            nameaddress.Email = '';
        }
    }

// ShipWithReturn() // returns void
this.ShipWithReturn = function () {
        vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = "RETURN SERVICE";
        vm.checkShip();
    }

// ShipNoReturn() // returns void
this.ShipNoReturn = function () {
        vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = "";
        vm.checkShip();
    }
